(Washington) US authorities have given coal industry workers until next Tuesday to agree to the coal industry's wage and hours regulations. Retail stores across the United States are now drafting regulations to set prices. (26th Reuters)

Stop Assisting Overseas Trading Firms

Major Change in US Commercial Policy

(Washington) The Department of Commerce and the State Department jointly announced today that, for economic reasons, they will stop assisting firms engaged in overseas commerce. This is a major change in US commercial policy. The assistance being discontinued includes conducting market research for various firms and negotiating or contacting affairs on behalf of firms, such as selling goods, concluding agency contracts, collecting debts, resolving commercial disputes, corresponding, or arranging face-to-face meetings between firms and foreign managers or buyers. (26th Reuters)

Shanghai-Philippines Test Flight Line Survey Completed

Scheduled to Fly Back to Shanghai on the 1st of Next Month

Manila Telegraph of the 26th: After Bixby, a representative of Pan American Airways, surveyed the Shanghai-Philippines air route, he is currently preparing a report to be sent to Pan American. He is scheduled to depart on September 1 and fly back to Shanghai. Today, Mr. Bixby declared that the plane will be able to fly south to Zamboanga. According to American news, someone will soon be exploring the South Pacific air route. Although it is not yet certain whether Pan American Airways will be conducting the exploration at that time, it is believed here that even if other companies are paying close attention to the Pacific air route, Pan American will undoubtedly be the first to explore it. It is believed that Mr. Bixby's trip to Zamboanga is sufficient to prove that Pan American may abandon the route from Honolulu via Midway Island, Wake Island, and Guam to Manila, and instead take the South Pacific route from Honolulu via Johnson Island, then west past various small islands to the Philippines. This is because some sections of the Guam route are no shorter than 1,200 miles, which is not as good as the South Pacific route, which has countless small islands for stops, which can reduce the amount of gasoline carried by the plane. It is also believed that if the Shanghai-Philippines air route extends south to Zamboanga after Manila, it may not be profitable. Mr. Bixby's visit to that place and detailed survey of the bays within a ten-mile radius that can be used for landing is related to the Pacific air route and is intended to take the South Pacific route. In addition, it is also heard that Pan American has abandoned the idea of taking the northernmost air route to China via Alaska, due to the dangerous weather conditions along the way.

Cuban Provisional President Begins to Exercise Authority

Orders Restoration of Old Constitution

Sets General Election for Next Spring

Dismisses Old Administrative and Judicial Officials

Generally Acknowledges International Debts

Reuters, Havana, 26th: The Cuban provisional government has begun to exercise its duties. Last night, Cuban provisional President Cespedes ordered the restoration of the 1901 constitution, dissolved the National Assembly, dismissed the governors of the provinces, criticized former President Machado for abuse of power, and declared that all measures taken by Machado while in office were illegal. The Cuban provisional government will still recognize the debts internationally concluded during the Machado era, but will dismiss all county magistrates and judges appointed by Machado. New elections have been scheduled for February 24, 1934.

Lindbergh Explores North Atlantic Route

Recognizes Importance of Shetland Islands

Reuters, Lerwick, Shetland Islands, 25th: According to Colonel Lindbergh's opinion, the Shetland Islands are located between Europe and America and can serve as an intermediate stop for flights between Europe and America. Their relationship is quite important and cannot be ignored. Today, Colonel Lindbergh drove to Sumburgh Head, the southernmost point of the mainland, to investigate the airfield there. Afterwards, he took a plane and circled for a week, and also inspected the life of the natives in the Bronze Age. Lindbergh paid special attention to the climate records of the area in recent years, and received a lot of materials from the British ship Chilwa, which was docked there. When asked when he would leave the island and what the second destination would be, Lindbergh did not reply, only saying that everything depends on the weather.

Various Groups in Shandong Request Investigation of Personnel Who Advocated Breaching the Dikes

Also Requesting Retention of One Million in National Taxes for Disaster Relief

Jinan Correspondence: Shandong Provincial Relief Association, Chamber of Commerce, Trade Association, Buddhist Association, Flood Relief Association and other organizations sent a telegram yesterday to Chairman Lin, President Wang, Chairman Chiang, as well as President of the Control Yuan Yu Youren and President of the Legislative Yuan Sun Ke, requesting that the personnel who advocated breaching the dikes be dismissed and investigated to appease public anger, and requesting that the Shandong Provincial Government retain one million yuan in national taxes to handle post-flood relief. The telegram reads as follows: "Chairman Lin of the Nanjing National Government, Premier Wang of the Executive Yuan, President Yu of the Control Yuan, President Sun of the Legislative Yuan, Chairman Chiang of the Military Commission, and members of the Relief Committee: The breach of the Yellow River in neighboring provinces has caused disaster in western Shandong, affecting more than a dozen counties, with more than two million casualties. Homes have been washed away, and people have lost their homes. Reports from various counties state that the dead have already been swept away by the waves, and the living are climbing trees for support, lacking food and clothing, and their safety is not guaranteed day and night. This is all the poison of the breaches in other provinces, resulting in countless tragic robberies along the river. The river water came suddenly, making the local area unable to prevent it. The solidity of the golden dikes was useless. The area of peace and happiness suddenly became a flooded country. The victims have no one to complain to, and the fish and turtles are pitiful. What is the intention of those who breached the dikes? They are not worthy of being eaten by dogs and pigs. They brazenly use neighboring countries as ditches. How can they face the residents? The culprits have been clamoring among the public, but the authorities have remained silent. Do they regard the fishermen as uncivilized people? Are they willing to use breaching the dikes as a contingency plan? Where are the regulations? Where does the law exist? In the late Qing Dynasty, whenever there was a breach of the Yellow River, those who failed to defend it were first dismissed and arrested to appease public anger. Now, the achievements of river management in various provinces are obvious to all. When the Yellow River floods, they are at a loss and openly send people to breach the dikes, causing the Yellow River to seize the Huai River's course, making western Shandong the tail end. Their intentions and actions are in line with the bandit Li Zicheng's approach of breaching the river to flood Kaifeng. Allowing such heinous and wicked culprits who endanger the country and harm the people to roam free outside the law, how can we talk about river works? How can we face the victims? How can we warn the future? How can we show the world? We should request the government to issue a clear order to dismiss and investigate the personnel who advocated breaching the dikes, to correct official corruption and comfort the victims, and to investigate and punish the officials responsible for river management who have failed in their duties, to show the government's sincerity in mending the fold after the sheep is lost and in distinguishing between good and evil. It is especially important to remember that the victims have suffered unexpected disasters. We humbly request that disaster relief funds be dispatched quickly to provide assistance. Please issue a clear order to the Shandong Provincial Government to temporarily allow the borrowing of one million yuan from the national tax revenue, including salt tax and tobacco and alcohol items, to quickly handle post-flood relief. We are extremely urgent in awaiting orders. Respectfully printed by representatives of the Shandong disaster victims: Zhao Xinru, Gu Zhujiu, He Supu of the Provincial Relief Association, Zhang Shuheng, He Shaojiang of the Chamber of Commerce, Shi Shaoxian, Miao Cun, Feng Nianlu of the Trade Association, Sha Yuebo, Lao Fuquan of the Buddhist Association, Han Luxiang, Zhu Jinggu, Wang Ziyu of the Western Shandong Flood Relief Association, and others. (25th)

A Travelogue of Chahar and Suiyuan

Vehicles on the PingSui Railway are Scarce and Passengers are Crowded

The Garrison at Qinglong Bridge Has Not Been Withdrawn, But Inspections Have Been Relaxed

The Journey from Zhangjiakou to Datong Takes Twelve Hours

A Certain Senior Military Officer Talks About the Bravery of Song's Army

Special Telegram from Suiyuan: During the tense situation in Chahar, the PingSui Railway was once interrupted. Now that Feng Yuxiang has left Chahar for Shandong and the Chahar issue has been resolved, the reporter is making a trip to Chahar and Suiyuan to investigate the truth about the Chahar issue and the situation in the Northwest. I departed from Ping on the 13th, first to Zhangjiakou, stayed for two days, then went to Datong to inspect, and then came to Suiyuan from Datong, arriving last night. The situation along the way is briefly recorded as follows:

When the reporter departed from Ping, the PingSui Railway had just been restored. Vehicles were scarce, passengers were crowded, and the journey was slow, with many delays. Between Ping and Zhang, inspections were slightly relaxed, and pedestrians had fewer scruples. However, the tracks were in disrepair and the vehicles were dilapidated. Being in the car was like riding a small boat into the sea, and I felt seasick. The bad state of the road administration can be imagined. Because of many events over the years, some have been destroyed, but no one has reorganized them.

At noon on the 13th, I boarded the train at Xizhimen, Beijing, and arrived at Nankou in three hours, which is the important gateway to the south of Juyongguan, hence the name. During the battles of the 15th year of the Republic, the Feng army and the Northwest army fought here, lasting half a year, which was a famous battle in the history of the Republic of China. After the war, the reporter visited the battlefield and found that the defense line was tens of miles long, and the trenches were meticulous and the fortifications were solid, which was the best of its time. Now, however, it is overgrown with weeds, and there is no trace of the battle. Only the towering monument to the fallen soldiers remains, leaving a scar on the bloody history of the civil war. When the train arrived at Nankou, it turned into the mountain road and changed to a large mountain train head, which was pushed up from the rear of the train and spiraled along the mountain road. I only saw thousands of mountains overlapping, with no end in sight. Crossing several mountains and passing through three or four caves, I arrived at Qinglong Bridge. When the Chahar situation was tense, the central armored train stayed here, heavily guarded, and inspected passengers. Now, although the soldiers have not been withdrawn, the inspection has been relaxed. The tracks here, due to the steep terrain, fold and go south, with the tracks in a Y shape, commonly known as the Y track. The direction of the vehicles also changes accordingly, making the tail the head, and continuing its work of climbing over mountains. Along the way, the mountains are high and the roads are dangerous. The Great Wall stands straight against the mountains, sometimes hidden and sometimes visible, like a divine dragon. The pass is majestic and naturally formed, truly one man guarding the pass, ten thousand men cannot pass. However, from here to the east, directly to Yuguan, the danger of the Great Wall remains the same, but the color of the rivers and mountains has changed early. Why is the natural barrier not enough to rely on? The train left Juyong and the terrain was slightly flatter, directly to Kangzhuang, which is the entrance to Kangzhuang Avenue, and went northwest for dozens of miles to Huailai. The city is surrounded by mountains, and the city walls stand on the top of the mountains, forming a natural fortress. When Pang Bingxun's troops entered Chahar, they once set up headquarters here to command various armies, and then from here to Shacheng. Now, it has been moved to Xuanhua, and the defense area is left to Feng Qinzai's troops. From Huailai to the northwest, passing through Shacheng, Xiahuayuan, Xinzhuangzi, and other places, these areas all became important areas during the period of resolving the Chahar issue. There are still relics of the fortifications along the road, and it is conceivable that the confrontation between the two sides was tense, with swords drawn and bows ready. It is still vivid in my mind. I arrived in Xuanhua at about eight o'clock in the evening. There are quite a few troops stationed in Xuanhua, in addition to Pang Bingxun's troops, as well as a part of Guan Linzheng's 25th Division, and Liu Zhendong's volunteer army of more than 2,000 people. The train stopped for half an hour and then headed west, arriving in Zhangjiakou when the clock struck ten. Zhangjiakou is the center of the Chahar provincial coup. I stayed in Zhang for two days and made some investigations.

At midnight on the 15th, I took a train from Zhangjiakou to continue westward, heading to Datong. From Zhangjiakou to Datong is only more than 300 miles, and there is no obstruction along the way, but it took as long as twelve hours, until twelve o'clock the next afternoon before arriving. The slowness of the train is truly strange. Datong is an important town in northern Shanxi, and also a famous scenic area in Shuofang. The Nine Dragon Stele and the Yungang Grottoes are ancient sites there. I stayed for two days,

and took a leisurely tour.

At 10:00 a.m. on the 18th, I boarded a train in Datong and traveled 90 miles, passing Fengzhen, and entered Suiyuan territory. Along the way, the mountains and hills are continuous and the grasslands are lush, which is a natural area for farming and animal husbandry. Unfortunately, due to inconvenient transportation and a sparse population, goods are abandoned on the ground and left to waste. After 3:00 p.m., I passed Zhuozishan. The train travels in the mountains, surrounded by mountains, which is a scenic spot. This mountain is a famous place outside the Great Wall, and ancient poems and essays praise it. Datong to Suiyuan is about 500 miles, and Zhuozishan is about halfway there. The train traveled for about six hours and arrived in Suiyuan. There was thunder and rain, so I took a short rest in the city.

On this trip to the west, I met a senior general who fought at Xifengkou in the same car. According to him, after the September 18th Incident, the three northeastern provinces fell into enemy hands. Song Zheyuan and Sun Dianying requested to send troops to recover the lost territory, advancing troops from Rehe, one route out of Chaoyang, and the other route out of Kailu, to meet in Shenyang. At that time, the national spirit in the Northeast was very strong. Even if they could not recover all the lost territory in one fell swoop, they could greatly frustrate the enemy's offensive. But it was not realized. Later, when the Japanese army plotted Rehe, Song again requested to enter Rehe and serve as the vanguard. Song served as the governor of Rehe in the 14th year of the Republic, and was familiar with the geography. Defending Rehe with him might not have been so unsavory. Even after Chengde fell and the Northeast Army fled into the Great Wall, they only received orders to reinforce the defense of Xifengkou. When they were about to advance, the Northeast Army was retreating. Everyone asked Song's troops what army they were and what they were going to do. They replied that they were the 29th Army and were going to resist the Japanese. The hearers all said that the enemy's forces were fierce, and not to mention the 29th Army, even the 99th Army would be difficult to resist. Song's troops heard this, scoffed, and marched 120 miles in a hurry to encounter the enemy. The soldiers were exhausted and there were no fortifications. They fought bravely and bloodily. Although they frustrated the enemy's offensive, they suffered more than 1,200 casualties. Later, the large army continued to arrive, all with the determination to fight the enemy to the death. After discussing with each other, they decided that their weapons were not as good as the enemy's. Rather than defending for a long time and being wounded, it would be better to go to the enemy and die on the battlefield. They rushed out from Panjiakou, Dongjiakou, and other places, killing into the enemy's line. The soldiers had a determination to die, and one soldier was equal to a hundred. They captured many enemies and the enemy's courage was chilled. After this battle, the enemy did not dare to look at them directly. Several times they took advantage of the emptiness to attack, but our army's actions were swift and agile, traveling 200 miles a day, responding as they came, and ultimately failed to succeed. After two months of stalemate, the Japanese army repeatedly attacked without success, and had great doubts. First, they did not know where the main force of Song's troops was. When they used planes to scout, they only saw a small number of troops stationed there. But when they attacked, they felt that the troops were strong and impregnable. Where was the main force? They never knew. Second, they did not know how many troops Song had. Song's defense line was very long, but no matter where the Japanese army attacked, there were strong troops responding, which could not be done with a small number of troops. As a result, the Japanese army felt that they did not know how many soldiers Song had. In fact, Song's troops on the front line only numbered tens of thousands, but they were used flexibly. Troops are valued for their quality, not their quantity. There is a reason for this. Now the Japanese army often uses Song's troops as a target for research, saying that Song's troops' weapons are not as good as the Japanese army's, and the rear transport is extremely inconvenient. What is the way to victory? It is worth studying. (Reached on August 19)

Songjiang

Bloody Incident Occurs in Shi Wu Tu

Wang Binggen, a villager from Shiwu Tu outside the North Gate, married Yin Quying. The relationship between the couple was initially harmonious, but recently, due to Wang Binggen's difficult livelihood, his wife had an affair with Gu Xiaodi. After Wang discovered this, he agreed to cede his wife, negotiating compensation of 150 yuan. After the contract was signed, Wang Binggen did not receive the money. Gao took it away in the middle. Wang regretted the agreement because of the price. Gu Xiaodi was unwilling to lose both his person and his money. Gu's friend Gu Songyuan and others secretly carried kitchen knives and went to Wang Binggen's house to make trouble last night. They disagreed with each other. Wang Binggen's shoulder was stabbed with a knife, and blood flowed like a column. The perpetrators fled one after another. It is said that this matter still needs to be negotiated.

[Nanhui]

Farmers Burn Bee Farm

Zhang Ziqing and others from Zhangjiazhai, Shenzhuang, founded the Zhoupu Bee Company, which has been in business for several years. Its bee farm is located near the house, with more than 150 boxes of bees. Recently, some busybodies spread rumors that the bees were flying into the fields, which was harmful to plants. The general farmers were suspicious. Unfortunately, there was heavy rain, and many of the yellow flowers that had opened in the fields and cotton fields fell off, which made them believe that it was caused by bee damage. They repeatedly negotiated with the farm and requested that the bee farm be moved elsewhere, but permission was not granted. The farmers gathered many people the night before last and suddenly burned all the beehives on the farm. The farm staff immediately flew to the Zhoupu Security Corps to report and request that the perpetrators be investigated. The corps immediately sent many corps soldiers to rush to the place, but they saw that there were thousands of farmers gathered, and the situation was tense. If they approached to investigate and arrest them, conflicts would inevitably occur, so they immediately returned to the corps to report. It is heard that the company's loss this time is estimated at more than 4,000 yuan.

Wuxi

On-site Examination of the Case of Murdering One's Husband

The case of Gu Zhang, a rural woman from Shangtang Village, Eighth District (Huai Xia City), colluding with her lover Sun Awu and her adoptive father Jin Enrong (i.e., Jin Kuilin) to murder her own husband, Gu Yinsheng, has been reported in this newspaper. At 7:30 a.m. yesterday (25th), Prosecutor Ren Guanghai of the County Court, along with a clerk, an inspector, and bailiffs, and escorting the adulterous woman Gu Zhang, took a pre-hired boat and were towed downstream by a Changshu ship. They arrived in the countryside at about 11:00 a.m. Prosecutor Ren and others went ashore and examined the scene of the crime at Gu Yunsheng's home. They then questioned Gu Zhang. According to her confession, Gu Yinsheng was killed by Sun Awu, Jin Enrong initiated the idea, and took the first action, and the body was dragged out from the gate. After the questioning, Prosecutor Ren went to the burial ground, ascended the public case, and again summoned Gu Zhang and Tupo Zhongying for questioning. He then instructed the Inspector Wang to conduct an on-site examination as required. The examination revealed two rope marks on the back of the deceased, one rope mark on the waist, two rope marks on the arms, one cloth strip mark on the left and right legs, and three hemp rope marks on the left and right hands, all of which were tied after death. There was a scratch on the neck, a thumbprint on the right side of the throat, and two or three finger marks on the face. The skin of the whole body was changed and the epidermis was peeled off. Both hands were bent forward and tied together. The urine and both eyes had rotted. It was confirmed that he had been strangled to death before his death. After the examination, he instructed the corpse's family to prepare a coffin for burial, and instructed Tupo to guard the two murder stones and the rope and cloth strips used to tie the corpse, which he ordered to be sent to the court the next day. They then returned by the original boat, arriving at the hospital at 8:20 p.m. As for the important criminal Jin Enrong, he was also transferred from the Public Security Bureau to the County Court yesterday (26th). After Prosecutor Ren opened the court for interrogation, Jin flatly denied that he had plotted to kill Gu Yinsheng. As a result, the court ordered him to be detained, pending the arrival of Sun and Gu for confrontation before further review.

Wujiang

Fugitive Gao Jinyu Apprehended

During the change of prison guards in April this year, Gao Jinyu, who had been sentenced to 15 years in prison and assigned to outside labor, escaped from the county prison. A wanted order was issued. After escaping from prison, the high-ranking criminal fled to Changxing, Zhejiang Province. On the 20th of this month, Gao was arrested for committing another crime. He was transferred to the Wujiang County Government for extradition on the 23rd and taken to the county for detention and sentencing.

Jiangyin

The Course of the Tax Police Regiment's Suppression of Bandits

Yilin Town, Funing, was looted by Zhang Zhigao's gang of hundreds of bandits with guns last month, and more than 100 civilian hostages were kidnapped. Li's Regiment of the 57th Division, Wang's Battalion of the Provincial Security Office, the Yancheng Anti-Smuggling Guerrilla Brigade, and the militia surrounded them in Majiadang. For more than ten days, it was not resolved. Later, Tang Shouzhi, battalion commander of the Second Battalion of the Fourth Tax Police Regiment, was ordered to assist in the suppression. On the 5th of this month, he departed from Jiangyin and arrived at Gujiazhuang, six miles away from Majiadang, on the 9th. He learned that the bandits had broken through the encirclement and fled to the northwest on the evening of the 8th. Battalion Commander Tang immediately led his troops to track them down. After three days and two nights, they surrounded the bandits at Wang'erzhuang, Lianshui County. After a day of fierce fighting and several charges, Wang'erzhuang was captured. At that time, 42 hostages were rescued, more than 100 bandits were killed, and dozens of rifles, muskets, and shotguns were seized and turned over to the regiment headquarters. In this battle, more than 60 officers and soldiers of the Second Battalion were killed or wounded.

Changzhou

County Government Executes Two Bandits by Firing Squad

The Wu Yi County Government, previously from the Ninth and Tenth Districts, brought in two bandit convicts, Ding Heshang and Zhu Pansheng. Interrogation revealed that the two convicts confessed to colluding with multiple individuals, wielding firearms, kidnapping Zhou Liu's foster child of the Xu surname, and obtaining ransom. Ding Heshang also confessed to robbing Chen Yugeng's home and fatally resisting the victim. They were sentenced to death, and the sentence was submitted to the Provincial Government for approval on the 25th. County Magistrate Cai immediately dispatched police to bring the two convicts to the court, verify their identities, and escort them to the Fengweidun execution ground for execution by firing squad.

Danyang

Local Militia Captures Bandits

The militia of the Tenth District of the county apprehended nine bandits, including Zhu Wangyou, in the Shuiguan Mountain area of Picheng. They also seized a handgun and four bullets. After interrogation by the militia, all confessed to planning a robbery in Shiqiaotou. They have been handed over to the county for interrogation and prosecution.

High Court President Visits Danyang for Inspection

Lin Biao, the President of the Jiangsu High Court, along with a court clerk, arrived in Danyang yesterday afternoon by car. They proceeded to inspect the county government prison. They were received by County Magistrate Guo, who inquired in detail about the Chongming case tried by Judge Xu Shichang and its current progress. Afterward, they lodged at the Lianhu Hotel, took a brief rest, and departed for the capital by train in the evening.

Yixing

Zhou Amao Meets a Tragic End

Three brothers, Zhou Genlin, Zhou Ahong, and Zhou Amao, from Changshu, had been residing in Fenghuangke, Shicha Township, Eighth District of Yixing County, for years. In June, Amao mistakenly caught fish belonging to a man surnamed Fu from Hunan. The dispute was mediated by the township office and did not escalate. On the morning of the 22nd of this month, at around 5 AM, Amao was herding ducks when Fu Wentang, Fu Wenke, and Fu Wenkui, along with their field hands Yu Yongfu and Sun Laosheng, pushed Amao to the ground, punched and kicked him severely, and threw him into a pond before leaving. Villagers rushed to help upon hearing the news, but he was already dead. His brother, Genlin, immediately reported to the Fifth Public Security Sub-Bureau. On the 23rd, Fu Wentang and Fu Wenke were apprehended and immediately sent to the General Bureau and then to the county for investigation. The county government dispatched personnel on the 24th to investigate and confirm that it was a case of murder. On the 26th, a strict order was issued to all police stations to swiftly arrest the fugitives Fu Wenkui, Yu Yongfu, and Sun Laosheng and bring them to justice for further investigation.

Zhenjiang

Yan Shaobo Suffers a Stench of Osmanthus Fragrance

Yan Shaobo, the owner of Yuantai Feng Rice Shop on Dagen Street in this city, had a dispute with a worker named Chen over wages. Yan, relying on his influence, suppressed Chen, who harbored resentment and sought revenge. Yesterday, Chen seized an opportunity to fill a straw bag with feces and, taking Yan Shaobo by surprise, suddenly put the bag over Yan's head, drenching him completely. The stench filled the air, and everyone held their noses. Chen, seeing his plan succeed, immediately fled.

Verdict on Counterfeit Cigarette Case

Zu Fugui and Wang Qikang, residents of Shengjia Lane in this city, were discovered by the Dadao Tobacco Company to be counterfeiting their Flying Tiger cigarettes. The company reported this to the Public Security Bureau, which arrested them. The court investigation concluded, and the case was transferred to the Criminal Court for trial on the 17th of this month. After closing arguments, the verdict was announced yesterday: Zu Fugui and Wang Qikang are each sentenced to two months imprisonment for counterfeiting trademarks and fined 200 yuan.

Yangzhou

Han Guojun and Others Telegraphically Oppose Wang Yingyu's Proposal

Since Wang Yingyu, Deputy Director of the Yellow River Commission, advocated using 500,000 yuan of unused funds from the Yangtze River flood control for the construction of a long seawall at the Yellow River estuary in Lu-Yu and the Tongwaxiang stone dam project, it has attracted considerable attention. Many have telegraphed to express their disapproval. It is now known that Mr. Han Zishi, a prominent figure in Jiangbei, also expressed his opposition to Wang's telegram. He specifically telegraphed Governor Gu of Jiangsu Province, requesting that the Executive Yuan consider the actual situation. Additionally, Dai Tianqiu and Bao Xiangzhong, executive and supervisory committee members of the Huai River Improvement Association, also expressed their opposition and separately telegraphed the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Interior, and the governors of Jiangsu, Shandong, and Henan, urging them to immediately instruct Wang to prioritize the allocation of funds from the Central Government to block the breaches and prevent further flooding and disaster.

Provincial Department Urges Land Tax Bureau to Build Yellow River Interception Dam

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, citing the impact of the Yellow River breach on canal transportation in Jiangbei counties, specifically telegraphed to each county, urging them to swiftly remit all collected but unremitted land taxes for canal transport to meet the needs of advance prevention. It is also known that the Canal Transport Bureau, to prevent the Yellow River from entering the Grand Canal, specifically telegraphed the Huai-Pi section to urgently construct a Yellow River interception dam in the Shunqing River area above Qingjiang, so that the Yellow River water flowing into the Central Canal would not flow into the Grand Canal. It is reported that the section, upon receiving the order, immediately mobilized laborers to rush the construction.

Nantong

Suppression of Bandits Fleeing Along the Jianghai Coast

In the coastal areas of Jiangbei, including Tonghai, Rugao, and Qidong, fishing households are currently in the peak season for catching jellyfish. However, bandits are causing disturbances at sea. Along the Maozhugang area of the Yangtze River, bandits are also intercepting merchant ships. Upon receiving reports, the Provincial Government ordered the fourth district commander of the Provincial Water Police to mobilize various teams and cooperate with the police and militias of each county to suppress the bandits.

Case of Colluding with Bandits Under the Pretext of Protecting Against Landslides

Feng Ziyun, a notorious bandit in Jiangbei, has been apprehended and executed. Last year, while this bandit was in Changyinsha, he colluded with Cui Hanxiang, using the pretext of protecting against riverbank landslides to recruit followers and purchase military supplies. When the case came to light, Cui fled. On the 25th, the suspect was captured in Pingchao and was handed over to the county government that evening for interrogation.

Jiaxing

Robbery and Assault at Wangjiawan

At the home of the Zhu family in Wangjiawan, south of Taojiaqiantang in Jiaxing, more than ten bandits armed with weapons suddenly broke into the inner room at midnight the day before yesterday, recklessly looting. Not satisfied, they used straw to burn Zhu's entire body, forcing him to reveal the location of hidden silver. Zhu fainted on the spot after being burned. After the robbers left, they went to a neighboring house to loot and injured the victims.

Hangzhou

Jianggan Kidnapping Case Solved

The case of the kidnapping of Sun Xiyun's three-year-old son, Hongwen, the owner of the Qianyuan Sugar Shop in Longshezui, Jianggan, Hangzhou, and the shooting death of the chauffeur Qian Jingchun, has been solved after half a month. A suspect named Cao Youcheng had been apprehended, but the interrogation yielded no clues. The Security Office of the Provincial Civil Affairs Department jointly offered a reward of 1,500 yuan for solving the case. Recently, the victim received a letter from the kidnappers demanding 50,000 yuan as a condition for the safe return of the child. The Provincial Public Security Bureau intensified the investigation and subsequently apprehended two female suspects, Guo Qinxian and Liu Asan, who confessed to participating in the conspiracy. They also identified Hong Quanmao, Jiang Jianqiu, Zhou Xin, Chen Zhaolin, Xue Wanli, and others as the kidnappers in the case. Yesterday, the Security Office, in conjunction with investigators, apprehended them at various locations, including Room 37 of the Huizhong Hotel in Xinshichang and Room 55 of the Hangzhou Hotel. The interrogation is currently underway.

Robbery Occurs Outside Qingtai Gate

The area outside Qingtai Gate in Hangzhou City is relatively remote. Yesterday (the 26th) at around 10 AM, Fang Jinfu, a native of Xiaoshan, came to Hangzhou to visit relatives. While passing through the area, two bandits wearing short blue cloth shirts and trousers, barefoot in cloth shoes, suddenly appeared, each holding a wooden imitation gun, and ordered him to remain silent. They robbed him of 18 silver dollars and 17 small silver coins. Afterward, Fang shouted for help. He Bingfu, a nearby farmer, heard the commotion and gathered a crowd by beating a gong, surrounding the bandits. The bandits fired three shots, injuring one farmer. One bandit managed to escape, while the other, Gao Yongfu, was captured on the spot and has been sent to the Security Office for interrogation.

Ningbo

Violent Gale Strikes Ningbo

Yesterday (the 24th) at 4:30 PM, Ningbo was suddenly hit by heavy rain, followed by a violent gale, which subsided after half an hour. More than 30 utility poles were blown down in the area from Xiancang Gate to North Gate. Many utility poles in the western and southern parts of the city were also blown down, causing the entire city to be without electricity. Last night, both inside and outside the city walls, it became a world of darkness. The Ningbo Public Security Bureau and the patrol brigades of various sub-bureaus, considering the vital importance of public safety, dispatched all personnel to patrol and strengthen security. The electric company, due to the excessive number of utility poles blown down, will be unable to restore power for four to five days.

Key figures from the Central Government are making preparations to welcome him in Shanghai. Sun Ke's Remarks Upon Returning to Shanghai

General Feng Will Enter the Capital to Take on Important Central Positions

Negotiations Underway to Obtain Feng's Consent Regarding His Title

Madam Sun Will Return to Her Hometown on the 30th

Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, along with Ma Chaojun and Fu Rulin, members of the Legislative Yuan, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing by night train at 8:00 AM yesterday morning. Our reporter interviewed Mr. Sun at his residence yesterday and recorded his remarks as follows:

(Feng Can Come to the Capital But Does Not Want to Stay Long) Mr. Sun first stated that he had a pleasant and productive meeting with Mr. Feng Huanzhang in Taishan. Feng was sincere in his attitude and indicated that he could visit the capital in the short term, but he does not wish to stay in the capital for long, as he is unaccustomed to city life. Regarding Feng's title, the Central Government intends to appoint him as Army Inspector or Water Conservancy Director, and they are currently seeking Feng's consent. Once Feng himself decides on which position he prefers, the official order will be issued. Ma Chaojun and Fu Rulin previously went to Lushan to meet with Chairman Chiang to discuss this matter, so there is no need for me to fly to Jiangxi again for the time being.

(No Change in Diplomatic Policy) Regarding the rumors widely spread by the Japanese side that our diplomatic policy has undergone a change, this can be disproven by the fact that Minister Song will not disembark in Japan on this trip. Although Wang Jingwei has assumed the position of Minister of Foreign Affairs concurrently, there is no intention to change the diplomatic policy for the time being. As for the claim that a secret loan of 80 million yuan has been made to Japan, not only does Japan not have the financial capacity for this, but our country is also unable to repay its previous Japanese debts, let alone take out another loan. Therefore, this kind of rumor is completely unfounded.

(Luo Wenkan's Inspection Consolidates the Border)

Foreign Minister Luo Wenkan's current inspection of Xinjiang is Luo's own idea. When the Central Government sent Huang Musong to Xinjiang, before his trip materialized, Luo already had this intention. However, at that time, due to the ceasefire in North China, he could not spare the time, and President Wang also believed that the diplomatic situation was tense and that he could not be without someone in charge, so he did not agree to Luo's trip, and the matter was dropped. Recently, because the diplomatic situation has come to an end, Luo made this request again, and the Central Government reluctantly approved it, in order to inspect the border situation and consolidate national defense.

(The Fifth National Congress Will Be Convened as Scheduled)

The Central Government is actively preparing for the Fifth National Congress. The Southwest opposes the convening of the congress, arguing that previous resolutions have not been fully implemented, and that there is no need to convene a congress in the future. This reason is not only unreasonable, but even ordinary organizations and institutions would not have such a superficial view, let alone this congress being the highest organ of the Party and the country. If the Guangdong Committee is dissatisfied with the failure to implement previous resolutions, it can take this opportunity to raise questions at the congress. If it only expresses dissatisfaction with the Central Government in the past, it may also submit its opinions to the congress for public discussion. Why oppose the convening of the congress? As for the claim that the Guangdong Province will convene another congress separately, it is just an attempt by a few people, and in reality, it is impossible. Some advocate that the congress should not be held in the capital, but in another location, but everyone knows that this is stipulated by the Party Constitution. If one does not recognize Nanjing as the capital, then it is clear that one is violating the Party Constitution.

(Staying in Shanghai to Wait for Song, Not Going to Guangdong for the Time Being) Mr. Sun finally stated that he came to Shanghai to take a break during the week and plans to stay in Shanghai to meet with Minister Song Ziwen before returning to Nanjing. As for the rumors that he will be going to Guangdong, they are inaccurate, and he has no intention of going south for the time being. According to sources close to Mr. Sun, Sun's mother, Madam Lu, is scheduled to return to her hometown on the 30th of this month, accompanied by Sun's son, traveling south by ship.

Kong Xiangxi Returned to Shanghai Yesterday

The Result of This Trip to Jiangxi to Meet Chiang Was Very Good

Madam Kong, Song Ailing, and Others Returned Together

Kong Xiangxi, the governor of the Central Bank, was invited by Chiang Kai-shek, chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, to travel by plane from Shanghai to Xun on Thursday of last week, where he then proceeded to Lushan to meet with Chiang to discuss important issues such as the Central Government's finances, the distribution of American cotton and wheat, and the rehabilitation of North China. A satisfactory conclusion was reached, and Kong left the mountain at 6:00 AM yesterday morning, transferring to Chiang Kai-shek's personal Stinson aircraft in Jiujiang. He departed from Xun at 8:00 AM and arrived in Nanjing at 12:00 PM, landing at Minggugong for a midday meal. At 3:00 PM in the afternoon, he boarded the same plane to fly to Shanghai, arriving safely at Hongqiao Airport at 4:30 PM. Kong and his entourage disembarked and returned directly to their private residence by car. The Sixth District Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau specially dispatched a squad of police officers to maintain order at the scene. Those who returned to Shanghai with Kong yesterday included his wife, Madame Song Ailing, their second daughter, Lingjun, their fourth son, Lingyi, and Secretary Tan and his bodyguards, totaling six people. After receiving the news, reporters from the Xinxin News Agency immediately drove to West Adams Road to visit and inquire about the details of this trip to Jiangxi. It was reported by his staff that the results of Kong's trip were very satisfactory.

Mayor Wu's Remarks Upon Returning to Shanghai

The Land Value Tax Must Be Collected, and the House Tax on Beisichuan Road Must Also Be Collected

Mayor Wu Tiecheng, who recently went to Nanjing on official business to meet with Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei and report on the city's recent municipal facilities, has now completed his mission and returned to Shanghai by train at 8:00 AM yesterday morning. At 10:30 AM, he met with reporters from various newspapers at the city government and made the following remarks regarding the city government's proposed land value tax and the collection of house tax on the encroached section of Beisichuan Road:

(Collecting Land Value Tax)

Wu first stated that the collection of the land value tax was a result of long-term consideration and planning, so it must be implemented. The reasons are as follows: 1. The tax burden on the people throughout the country is lightest in Shanghai, especially for the citizens in the urban area. According to the obligations of citizens to the country, they must not hesitate or shirk their responsibilities.

(Average Burden)

2. In the urban area, even in the residential area, the land value in Nanshi and Zhabei ranges from several thousand taels to more than ten thousand taels per mu, which is very different from the land value in the rural areas of Wusong, Jiangwan, Caohejing, and Hongqiao Town, which ranges from two to three hundred yuan to four to five hundred yuan per mu. The rental income in Nanshi and Zhabei is many times higher than the crop yields in Wusong, Jiangwan, and other places, but the taxes levied on houses, land, and fields in the past were almost the same, which is extremely unfair.

(Taxing the Rich More)

The Chinese rural economy is deteriorating, which is also due to the excessive burden on farmers. As for the landlords' so-called burden of paying house tax, it should be noted that the house tax is mainly used for police affairs. In short, those who oppose it can continue to make excuses, but I dare to say frankly that taxes should be levied more on the rich and not harshly demanded from the poor. Therefore, the collection of the land value tax must not be delayed, and there is no possibility of delay. The city's revenue should be based on the principle of living within one's means. What is necessary for municipal construction must be implemented resolutely and as soon as possible, because it is of a dead nature rather than a living one. After the city government completes the preparatory work, it will immediately begin to collect the tax from the residential area according to law, with an estimated annual income of more than one million yuan, which will be used entirely for municipal construction.

(House Tax Must Be Collected)

Wu continued that the house tax on the encroached section of Beisichuan Road must not be accommodated again and must be strictly enforced according to law. The merchants in the area want to request a delay in the collection again, which is unreasonable. They make excuses that the area is encroached and want to wait until the negotiations are completed before starting the collection, which is even more insane. They are Chinese people living on Chinese land. Even for concessions, concessions are on other people's land and will still be our country's territory when the term expires. Therefore, its sacred judicial power is still in our hands, and the First and Second Special District Courts are established. It is only that part of the prosecutorial power is subject to certain restrictions. Now they are not living in a concession but in an encroached area in a purely Chinese area, enjoying the benefits of municipal facilities. How can they not have the obligation to pay taxes? The city government should persuade them on one hand and strictly enforce the collection on the other hand.

A Citywide Market Strike Occurred in Luodian Yesterday

The District Chief Forbids the Employment of Specialists to Collect Debts

The Business Community Adopts Passive Resistance

A citywide market strike suddenly broke out in Luodian Town in Baoshan County yesterday. The situation is detailed below:

Reasons for the Strike Luodian Town is the first major town on the entire Hutai Road. Its surrounding villages are as far as six or seven li, more than ten li, or even twenty li away. Therefore, the market is more prosperous than Liuhe Town in Taicang County. The debts owed to the shops are not only inconvenient to collect due to the long distance, but there are also stubborn and impoverished debtors who have been in arrears for three to five years or even six to seven years. Therefore, shops in the town have the practice of hiring specialists to collect debts in the villages. Recently, the Fourth District Affairs Conference decided to prohibit shops from hiring opium addicts and beggars to collect debts and presented it to the county government for approval. Notices were issued to prohibit this. Shops were panicked because they would have no way to collect debts in the future. The afternoon before yesterday, at around 3:00 PM, they went to the town's chamber of commerce to hold a meeting to discuss countermeasures. They dispersed at 2:00 AM without any results. As a result, yesterday, the entire town went on strike.

Reasons for the Strike After the town went on strike, it issued the reasons for the strike, stating that a market strike is originally a passive resistance method. Otherwise, who would dare to act rashly and sacrifice themselves? This time, Wang Qingshou, the district chief of the Fourth District Office of the town, arbitrarily based his proposal on the vague proposals of the village chiefs in the District Affairs Conference and presented it to the county government for instructions. There was no consultation beforehand and no guarantee afterward. It provides convenient opportunities for debtors and makes it impossible for creditors to collect debts. Therefore, the government is using its power to oppress the business community, and the business community will not accept it. Since receiving the county government's instructions, the merchants have felt a significant obstruction and impact on the collection of debts. When the general meeting was held yesterday, District Chief Wang was respectfully invited to attend and provide guidance on rescue measures. However, he continued to perfunctorily answer, and his tone implied that the merchants were indiscriminately lending debts, resulting in uncollectible debts. After deliberating for half the night, there was no result, so they finally decided on this last resort of a market strike. The following is a list of what the merchants are demanding:

Merchants' Demands 1. The resolution passed by the District Affairs Conference, which restricts merchants from hiring people to collect debts, should be completely overturned, and the county government should be requested to withdraw its order. 2. None of the dozens of village chiefs in each village is not in arrears with the shops (only one or two are not in arrears). This time, the village chiefs sponsored this resolution for their own selfish purposes. It is now necessary to order each of the village chiefs to first pay off all the debts to the shops in full as an example, otherwise, these stubborn village chiefs should be removed. 3. Sun Yingfeng, assistant to the Fourth District Office, is just a young man with no knowledge or skills and should be dismissed. 4. The district office itself has been in arrears with the shops for years and has never paid them back. This time, it is also requested to pay them back in full to avoid default. The above points are the common demands of the merchants of the entire town.

Chamber of Commerce's Submission Wang Daxun, acting chairman of the Luodian Chamber of Commerce, submitted a document to the county government yesterday, requesting an urgent telegram report. The document states: According to the instructions of your government, Wang Qingtao, the district chief of the Fourth District, presented a request to ban merchants from collecting debts, etc. While this was being reviewed and forwarded, the entire town's merchants came to the association to hold a meeting, stating that District Chief Wang not only does not prohibit the villagers from buying on credit but also prohibits the merchants from collecting debts and falsely accuses them of hiring beggars and opium addicts to prohibit them from collecting debts, which is tantamount to condemning the merchants to death. It is requested that District Chief Wang consider the difficulties of the merchants and withdraw the original report. District Chief Wang then stated that he was not present at the District Affairs Conference at the time and was not familiar with the details of the case. He will meet with the county magistrate to discuss a solution. The merchants were not satisfied with the district chief's vague words, so they decided to suspend business and wait for orders. In an instant, the entire town went on strike. This case was revived from an old case of the District Affairs Conference, which led to the repeat of the evil drama of September 18, 1931. The district chief regretted not knowing the details, and the association was ashamed that it could not mediate. They are now doing their best to persuade them together with the Public Security Bureau, but it has no effect. It is urgently reported to County Magistrate Jin of Baoshan County for review and approval, and a suitable person should be sent to Luodian to guide them, which is extremely urgent. Respectfully presented.

Post-Strike Inspection After learning of the above situation, the reporter went to inspect the entire town and saw that each shop had posted slogans condemning the District Affairs Conference for oppressing the merchants and forcing them to go on strike. There were also various red and green slogans at other bridgeheads and alleys, with very激烈 words omitted. All the shops, including food shops, were closed, which was even quieter than the Lunar New Year. When returning to Shanghai, it was also heard that the county government had sent Zhang Qian, the chief of the Public Security Section, Chen Jiamo, a member of the County Party Department Reorganization Committee, and Liu Shouquan, a party affairs member, to Luodian to mediate.

The Collection of House Tax on Beisichuan Road Has Been Successfully Resolved

House Tax Will Still Be Collected Starting This Autumn

The City Government Approves the Allocation of 10,000 Yuan in Relief Funds

The city government had previously announced that the house tax on the encroached section of Beisichuan Road would be collected starting this autumn. The merchants in the area requested a delay in implementation due to the slow recovery after the war, which has not been resolved. Recently, Wen Hongen, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, came forward to mediate and decided on three measures: 1. The house tax will be collected starting this autumn. 2. The city government will allocate 10,000 yuan from the house tax to serve as war relief funds for the area. 3. The distribution of the relief funds will be subject to the opinions of the citizens of the area and will be implemented with the approval of the city government. The city government has approved it, and the citizens have expressed satisfaction, and the case has been successfully resolved.

The Anti-War Association Contacts Meeting Venues After Malais Returns to Shanghai

A Heartfelt Discussion on Impressions of Traveling in Japan

According to the Huadong News Agency, Lord Marley, Chairman of the World Anti-War Association and former Under-Secretary of State for War of the United Kingdom, recently arrived in Shanghai with five representatives from the European Anti-War Association. They then went to Japan with Dr. D. Marteau, the French representative, hoping that Japan would send a representative to the association to eliminate the clouds of war in the world. Unexpectedly, as soon as Mr. Marley arrived in Kobe, he was monitored by the Japanese military police authorities and questioned for four hours. He was also forbidden to meet with Army Minister Araki and the British consuls in Japan, and was restricted to returning to Shanghai on the same day. During the questioning, Kobe frequently notified Tokyo by telephone for further questioning. Although they were not threatened, they were overwhelmed by the harassment. The two quietly returned to Shanghai the day before yesterday and checked into the Cathay Hotel. A reporter from the Huadong News Agency specifically inquired about the news from the association yesterday, which is recorded as follows:

(Japanese Interrogation) According to Mr. Marley, he arrived in Kobe on August 21. At that time, a large number of representatives from the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, military police, authorities, and the press were talking to each other. From 8 a.m. to 1 p.m., questioners came continuously. During the questioning, Mr. Marley said that he was not a communist. Communism could be practiced in one country, but not in another, depending on the circumstances. The purpose of his visit to Japan was to ask the British Embassy to request the Japanese authorities and Army Minister Araki to allow

Page 14

Japanese representatives to attend the Anti-War Association. At that time, the Japanese told him that there was a Japanese person who could sympathize with the Anti-War Association, named Kanju Kato, who currently lives in Shanghai.

(Strict Search of Luggage)

Mr. Marley was never able to speak with the British consuls in Japan. Most of the representatives from the industrial and labor sectors who came to see him were also prohibited. Several books left in his suitcase were mostly detained. One of them was "Tanaka's Positive Manchurian Invasion Memorial," which Mr. Marley had prepared for the Anti-War Association for reference, and was also searched and taken away.

(Actively Preparing for War) Mr. Marley made an affirmative statement about the situation of actively preparing for war. He said, "The Japanese authorities are afraid of us entering the country because they know the importance and influence of the anti-war movement. Although they are now actively preparing for war, they also have to

hesitate. Moreover, their industry is already very developed, but the supply of raw materials is lacking, and the domestic market is too small, so the national situation is extremely turbulent and tense. It is expected that they will seek a way out through war." Mr. Marley also said that Japan is preparing for war, so it is very xenophobic, especially towards the British and Americans. Once they enter the country, they will be strictly monitored. Therefore, opposing imperialism and war is a matter of urgency.

(Foreign Newspaper Records) The Great American Evening News said that Lord Marley, the leader of the Anti-War Conference representatives, visited Mr. Peel, the Director-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council, and Mr. Fessenden, the President, today (26th). Afterwards, according to Mr. Marley, the visit today was of a social nature, just an ordinary conversation. According to his impression, the attitude of the Director-General of the Municipal Council towards the purpose of the association can be said to be completely without prejudice. He told Mr. Peel that the representatives had not yet decided on the matter of requesting a meeting in the Public Concession, because the place of the meeting could not be decided until the relevant factors, such as the attitude of the Chinese government towards the meeting, the number of participants, and the general nature of the meeting, had been considered again. Mr. Marley said that he would visit the French Consul-General and the Mayor of Shanghai, Wu Tiecheng, at the beginning of next week, or possibly on Monday, but this visit would be of the same nature as today's visit to Mr. Peel. Mr. Marley continued that Mr. Peel had stated that the Municipal Council sympathized with the meeting on the one hand, but on the other hand, the possibility of disturbances must also be considered. Finally, he thanked Mr. Peel for the safety of the representatives by the Municipal Council. According to reports, after Mr. Marley returned to Shanghai from Japan yesterday, the Public Concession Police Department immediately granted his request and sent two detectives for special protection. As for the representatives attending, it is reported that Qilu University in Jinan recently requested to send a representative to the meeting, and the British representative, Hamilton, replied with a welcome telegram.

More than 30 Japanese soldiers were killed, 17 were captured, and one enemy commander, Captain Sasaki Yoshi, was killed. Two mortars, four machine guns, and a lot of rifles and bullets were seized. The Japanese army retreated to the Feketu River, 80 li west of Bin County, to defend, and there is no sign of a counterattack. The battle lasted for two days and nights, and the street fighting lasted for more than ten hours. About 170 members of the Righteous Army and about 30 civilians died. During the street fighting, Japanese aircraft assisted in the battle, destroying the county town with artillery fire. Ministry of Communications Mediates the Post Office Layoff Dispute

Layoffs Changed to Retirement with Two Months' Salary

The Shanghai Postal Workers' Union and the Postal Employees' Union opposed the postal authorities' decision to forcibly lay off more than 30 senior personnel nationwide from September 1st this year, which violated the Postal Regulations, causing opposition from postal workers in various places. It is now learned that in order to avoid the expansion of the situation, the Ministry of Communications has accepted the principle and proposed two mediation methods: 1) Change the layoffs to voluntary retirement; 2) Give another month's salary. After receiving the telegram from the Ministry, the two associations convened a joint meeting of all executive supervisors yesterday. First, Chairman Zhang Kechang reported on the negotiation process, and then the mediation methods were proposed for discussion. As a result, it was decided that 1) In principle, the purpose of canceling the layoffs has been achieved, and it should be changed to voluntary retirement. The mediation methods should be ordered to be checked by the relevant employees.

2) Submit to the General Assembly for record. At the beginning of this incident, the two associations suggested to the General Bureau to give it due consideration, but because the Director Huang Naishu's attitude was tough and he firmly refused to accept it, a deadlock was formed. Now, with the sincere mediation of the Ministry of Communications, the dispute can be said to have been resolved.

Telegram Requesting Relief for Hundreds of Thousands of Disaster Victims

The Shanghai Charity Organizations Joint Relief Association for Northeastern Refugees received a telegram from the Hebei Relief Committee yesterday, saying that the charitable organizations are all aware that Hebei is unfortunately plagued by disasters. The war has just ended, and the floods have followed. Since July of this year, the Daqing, Tuo, Zhu, Ji, Yun, Zhang, Wei, and other rivers have successively burst their banks. All the dikes have collapsed. Anping, Raoyang, Boye, Daming, Jixian, Lixian, Di, Changcheng, and other ten counties have all become swamps. Preparations for relief are underway, but the Yellow River has burst its banks again within the Changyuan territory. The torrent is surging, and Changyuan, Dongming, and Puyang counties are all sighing. The suffering is even worse than the above-mentioned counties. According to telegrams from the counties, the water is more than ten feet deep, endangering the city walls. Villages and houses have been washed away, and people and animals have drowned. Those who are fortunate enough to survive are escaping to trees and crying for help. The situation is unbearable to see. The flood in Changyuan is particularly large and has already entered the city. The severity of the disaster is no less than the water disasters in Jianghuai last year. At present, Puyang, Yuan, and Dong counties have already distributed urgent relief in advance, but the disaster is too serious, and it is only a drop in the bucket. It is difficult to provide a complete life without continuing to raise huge sums of money. Although the disaster in Daming, Anping, and other ten counties is slightly lighter than the former three counties, the disaster area is vast and the number of disaster victims is large. They are all hungry and look forward to relief. Without planning a large amount of relief funds and distributing them separately, it is difficult to extend the remaining life. The association is responsible for relief and cannot shirk its responsibility. However, after the great disaster, the financial situation is exhausted, and the treasury is empty. It is a pity that we lack the art of turning stone into gold. We are wandering around in a panic and have no策. Moreover, during the water disasters in Jianghuai last year and the war in North China this year, the central government and various parties provided huge sums of money or provided clothing and medicine. Righteous grain and benevolent slurry have saved countless lives. The water disasters suffered by Changyuan and other counties are the same as the above-mentioned soldiers and water disasters. We earnestly request you to be mindful of the people's difficulties and give early and generous relief, so that hundreds of thousands of hungry people on the river bank can enjoy the rain and dew. May the benefits to the disaster victims be endless. The telegram is extremely urgent and awaits orders. The following is omitted.

The Pudong Association Sends a Telegram Requesting Not to Add Two Yuan to the Winter Grain Tax

How Can a Political System Be Credible If It Breaks Faith with the People?

Regarding the issue of Jiangsu Province adding two yuan to the winter grain tax, the Pudong Association held a meeting of directors and supervisors a few days ago and decided to send a telegram to the Central Government, saying that the Jiangsu Province's addition of two yuan to the winter grain tax has been repeatedly presented by local groups since the 19th year. The Ministry of Finance approved that this case would be limited to the winter grain tax in the 19th year. However, it continued to be levied in the 20th and 21st years. At the beginning of the 21st year, the association presented a telegram to the Ministry of Finance with the serial number Fu Zi 284, stating that starting from the 21st year, the order of the Executive Yuan to exempt the tax would be followed. However, the tax was still levied in December. A telegram was presented to the Ministry of Finance with the serial number Fu Zi 989, stating that the two yuan added to the winter grain tax this year was previously approved by the Executive Yuan. It seems that year after year, the government has broken faith with the people. How can such a political system be credible? Now it is heard that the Jiangsu Provincial Government has submitted a proposal to continue levying the tax, and the public is terrified. It is not only the association that feels this way. At a time when rural areas are bankrupt, talking about revitalization is better than reducing extra demands. The country is based on the people. Cherishing one point of the people's strength is cultivating one point of vitality. If there is a proposal to extend the tax, please do not approve it. We are extremely eager to await orders. The Pudong Association bows and begs for forgiveness.

Minutes of the Meeting of the Shanghai Branch of the Engineers' Association

The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Institute of Engineers held a regular meeting at the Bankers' Club at No. 4 Hong Kong Road at 7 p.m. on the 21st. About 20 people attended. The meeting was chaired by Vice President Wang Shengshan. The meeting first gathered for dinner. After dinner, Dai Ji, a member of the association and a lacquer expert, gave a speech on the progress of lacquer technology in the past 25 years, such as the application of electronic methods, the use of tung oil instead of flaxseed oil, and the improvement of lacquer manufacturing machinery. The most labor-saving and time-saving lacquer manufacturing machinery can now be managed by one person, and can produce lacquer cans by mechanically feeding materials for a certain period of time, and can produce various styles. However, its most important raw material is tung oil. Countries have been using tung oil produced in China for many years, and they are now engaged in planting tung trees in their own countries and have achieved results. Although the output is not much at present, each country will be able to supply itself in the future. At this time, China must quickly prepare for it and use other methods to make oil with a lower value to replace tung oil, such as the example of using both real silk and rayon. Mr. Dai's research on manufacturing tung oil using machine oil has been successful and can be called artificial tung oil to meet future needs. The attendees discussed it, and Chairman Wang expressed his thanks and said that China's lacquer industry was originally a major industry, but since the import of foreign lacquer, many Chinese people have used foreign lacquer, so a lot of money has been leaked out every year. In recent years, Mr. Dai Ji and his colleagues have advocated the self-manufacture of foreign lacquer, and several factories have been established. After several years of competition with foreign imports, they have now regained 60% of the foreign goods sales. Such management can be said to be the right way to save the country, and I am deeply impressed. The meeting was adjourned at more than 10 o'clock.

The Shanghai National Goods Factory Union sent a letter to each factory yesterday, saying that the personnel situation has become increasingly complicated in recent years, and factories have felt more and more difficulties in management. The union, in view of this, consulted with Shanghai University last summer and jointly established an industrial management training class in the School of Commerce of the university. All students are recommended by various factories and graduate in one year. The curriculum focuses on factory management accounting and various industrial regulations. The teachers are drawn from the teachers of the School of Commerce and rotate to teach. For the past year, the results have been remarkable. Minutes of the Meeting of the Rice Milling Industry Association

Resolving on Machinist Prices

The Rice Milling Industry Association held a special meeting yesterday, chaired by Zhu Zixiang. It was resolved that the machinist prices in the industry were inconsistent. It is now stipulated that starting from September 1st, the customer cargo buns transported to Shanghai will be 155 catties (including the bag) per Shanghai peck, 21 cents per Shanghai peck for rough indica rice, 23 cents for rough japonica rice, 25 cents for rough yuan rice, and 16 cents for turned rice. In addition, the factory is prone to losses if the customer cargo remittance and transport to Shanghai cannot meet the prescribed limits. It was decided that the association should notify the Nanjing Silver and Money Association and the Transportation Industry Association to follow the prices set by the conference. If the prices are exceeded, the industry will unanimously refuse to mention it. The prices set will be notified once a week, and a committee to determine the limit prices will be appointed. In addition, the association will send a letter questioning the stone powder factory's joint price increase. Since the price of rice has fallen drastically and new measuring instruments have been used, the price should be reduced and should not be increased. If the price increase cannot be canceled, the industry will not adopt it. Other cases were discussed and the meeting adjourned.
