Rickshaw Puller Couldn't Bear the Pain and Committed Suicide by Poisoning

Sun Shaoqing, a rickshaw puller from Jiangbei, 53 years old, lived in the Yang's rickshaw inn (commonly known as a rickshaw den) at No. 12 Saint Trinity Road, French Concession. Recently, he suffered from illness, and the treatment was ineffective. He endured a lot of pain and had a short-sighted idea. He swallowed raw opium and committed suicide the day before yesterday. When the poison took effect, the innkeeper, Yang, realized that he had suffered from heatstroke. After inquiring, he learned that he had committed suicide by poisoning because of his illness. He was rushed to Renji Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective. He died at 6:50 a.m. yesterday. The hospital notified the French Police Station, and the police sent a detective to take the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Mortuary for an autopsy. In the morning, the Chief Prosecutor of the Second Special District Court, Chen Beisan, arrived at the mortuary and confirmed that the deceased had committed suicide by poisoning before his death. Because the body belonged to a poor man who could not afford a coffin, the court approved the body to be buried by Tongren Fuyuan Hall on his behalf.

A Truck Crushed a 71-Year-Old Man

Liu Huai-shu Dies Tragically

Liu Huai-shu, an elderly Jiangbei vegetable vendor residing in a thatched cottage on Bailinan Road in West Shanghai, aged 71, was selling vegetables in front of the Minsheng Factory in Zhoujiaqiao market at approximately 6:10 am yesterday when a cargo truck with license number 3702, traveling slowly from west to east, approached. As the old man attempted to move out of the way, the Minsheng Factory released its workers, causing a surge that knocked him to the ground. The truck's rear wheel ran over his head, instantly shattering his skull, splattering his brain matter, and causing his immediate death. The scene was gruesome and unbearable to witness. A police officer on duty arrived and detained the driver, Zhang Ziyun, along with the truck in the Sixth District. The officer then instructed the local bailiff to report the incident to the District Court Prosecutor for inspection. The bailiff ordered the deceased's son, Mingzi, to prepare for the encoffining and burial. After an interrogation by District Officer Jiang, the driver was sent to the General Bureau for further investigation.

Page 15

Autopsy of Bullet Proves Huang Yonghua Was Killed by Communists

Bullet identical to the one used in the assassination of Ma Shaowu

The bandits planned meticulously in advance and had been scouting for days

| Huang Yongquan, Huang's attendant, also died of severe injuries last night |

Huang Yonghua, Director of the Special Affairs Section of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's Inspection Department, was shot and assassinated by two thugs near the elevator on the fifth floor of the New Shanghai Hotel on Nanjing Road in the Public Concession at approximately 11 p.m. the night before. Huang was hit by two bullets and died on the spot. Huang's attendant, Huang Yongquan, was also seriously injured. Details were previously reported in this newspaper. After the incident, the Lao Zha Police Station immediately transported Huang's body to the forensic examination center on Ferren Road to await autopsy. They also urgently notified Director Wen of the Public Security Bureau by telephone, who promptly dispatched Detective Captain Lu Ying and all detectives to investigate. At the same time, detectives from the Lao Zha Police Station thoroughly examined the bullet casings, and the results indicated that they were the same as the bullets used in the recent assassination of former Inspectorate Special Affairs Director Ma Shaowu, proving a complete connection to the Ma case.

(Corpse Examination) Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo Wei, dispatched by the First Special District Court, arrived at the forensic examination center to inspect the body. In the opening statement, the Western police chief explained the investigation process, stating that three bullets and four bullet casings were found at the scene of the incident. Public Security Bureau Inspector Wang Wenjun added that the deceased's family members were all in their hometown, so Director Wen sent him to claim the body on their behalf. Prosecutor Guo, after hearing the testimony, ruled that the deceased Huang Yonghua had died from gunshot wounds to the abdomen. The three bullets and four bullet casings were temporarily handed over to the police station's firearms department for examination. The escaped murderers were to be strictly apprehended by the police for investigation and prosecution. The body was handed over to Wang Wenjun, the representative of the Public Security Bureau, who signed for it and took it away for encoffining and burial.

(Successive Important Positions) Yesterday, this reporter spoke with a close friend of Huang, a current Public Security Bureau official. According to him, Huang's true hometown was Rugao, Jiangbei, but he falsely claimed to be from Shaoxing due to special foreign connections. It was also said that Huang Yonghua was not his real name. He had indeed joined the Communist Party at one time and held a special position within the party. When he was in his hometown, he had several disputes with the Rugao County Party Committee. At that time, Huang resolutely changed course and surrendered to the Central Government, becoming a loyal comrade of the Chinese Nationalist Party. Subsequently, he successively held important positions such as Director of the Political Training Department of the 28th Division of the 31st Army of the National Revolutionary Army, Staff Member of the Training Department of the Central Party Headquarters, Judge of the Military Law Department of the Wuhan Headquarters of the Commander-in-Chief, Special Commissioner of Party Affairs of the 12th Division of the Army, and Staff Member of the Organization of the Central Party Headquarters. On September 26 of last year, he was appointed by the Central Government as a preparatory committee member of the Seamen's Special Party Department. On November 9 of last year, he was appointed Director of the Special Affairs Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. The previously assassinated Ma Shaowu was Huang's assistant.

(Usual Precautions) In recent years, most of the reactionary organizations uncovered in Shanghai were handled by Huang. Therefore, the Communist Party held a grudge against him, and Huang was well aware of his dangerous situation. Although Huang's residence was in the Chinese area, only one or two direct superiors and perhaps his closest friends and relatives knew of its location. Even when important matters occurred, he only communicated by telephone, which shows a glimpse of his daily precautions. Huang went to Beijing on the 20th of this month for important late-night matters and arrived in Shanghai on the early morning express train at 7:30 a.m. the day before yesterday. He immediately took his own car, number 8085 (Chinese area number 2289), directly to his residence. Because Huang's wife, Zhou Lanzhen, had gone to a retreat in Hangzhou's West Lake to recuperate, he left after a short stay.

(Bandits' Plans) It was not until around 10 p.m. that he went to Room 618 on the fifth floor of the New Shanghai Hotel to meet a friend, unaware that the bandits had been lying in wait. According to a tea server at the New Shanghai Hotel, around 2 p.m. the day before yesterday (the 22nd), a male guest speaking with an Anhui accent, wearing a dark blue silk shirt, and about 30 years old, came to the hotel and booked Room 519 on the fifth floor under the surname Gao. Soon after, two men in short blue outfits arrived and talked behind closed doors for a long time, acting very suspiciously. They never called a tea server into the room. The next day, they changed to Room 638 on the south side of the fifth floor, and three more men, one in a gray long gown and two in white silk long gowns, came to visit and talked for a long time before leaving. After Huang's tragic incident, these unwelcome guests left and never returned.

(Central Government's Condolences) The assassins' procedures were very thorough. Since Ma Shaowu's death, Huang had been constantly on edge, taking precautions everywhere. Whenever Huang went to a place, he would first hold his self-defense pistol in his hand and inspect the surroundings before getting in or out of a car. Unexpectedly, the bandits had thoroughly scouted his movements and assassinated him by shooting near the elevator on the fifth floor, a place no one would have expected. This shows that they had a detailed plan in advance. The Central Government was extremely saddened by Huang's tragic death. His body has been encoffined at the China Funeral Home. The funeral expenses, which will cost over 1,000 yuan, will be advanced by Director Wen.

(Attendant's Death) In addition to his wife, Zhou, Huang also had an elderly mother in her seventies and a five-year-old daughter. His family situation is very desolate. Huang's attendant, Huang Yongquan, after being sent to Renji Hospital, died at 9 p.m. last night because the bullet had pierced a vital part of his chest. Although the doctors tried their best to save him, he died due to excessive bleeding from the lung injury. The hospital notified the police station, who transported the body to the forensic examination center on Ferren Road to await autopsy.

Box Corpse Case: Suspect Admits to Murder During Preliminary Hearing

Appears calm and shows no fear

Elder brother is terrified and denies everything

| Suspect to be handed over to Macao after another round of witness questioning |

Yesterday morning, the Portuguese Consulate held its fourth hearing on the box corpse case. The suspect, Ba Delie, was subjected to three preliminary hearings, and all the witnesses appeared in court, proving his criminal behavior. The Portuguese suspect, realizing that he could not deny the charges, confessed in court to killing the Cantonese woman Zhang Cailian. At this point, the truth of the case was revealed. The Portuguese Consulate's investigation of this case lasted fifteen days and included four preliminary hearings, and it can now be considered complete. The details of yesterday's hearing and the suspect's confession are recorded below.

(All Witnesses Gathered) The Portuguese Consulate's interrogation in the box corpse case was entirely dependent on the witnesses appearing in court to testify, making it impossible for the suspect to deny the charges. At 10:30 a.m. yesterday, Portuguese Consul-General Dr. Xue Erfo brought the defendants Ba Delie Leimidao and Qiu Shifu Leimidao.

All the witnesses in the case were present, including the landlord of No. 15 Jiaxing Road, Chen Chunyuan from the Zongpeng store on Jiaxing Road who sold the iron bed, his partner Ma Xiaowei, the Japanese neighbor Da Cang from No. 14 Youyifangli, and the Portuguese, etc. Linghua Photo Studio, which took Zhang Cailian's photo, also sent Zhao Bingkun to court. With all the witnesses gathered, the Portuguese Consul began the interrogation.

(Municipal Government Sends Observer) The Shanghai Municipal Government sent Counselor Luo Panhui to court to observe during the first interrogation by the Portuguese Consulate. Yesterday's fourth preliminary hearing marked the end of the interrogations in Shanghai, so Counselor Luo came to the Portuguese Consulate with a letter to observe before the court session began and remained until the interrogation was completed. The lawyer hired by the defendant, Lei Gelun, also appeared in court to defend Ba Delie and Qiu Shifu. Therefore, yesterday's interrogation had more witnesses than the previous three hearings.

(Suspect Confesses to Brutal Murder) The suspects Ba Delie and Qiu Shifu were escorted to court by Western Detective Williams from the police station at 10:40 a.m. and remained seated in the defendant's dock. The Portuguese Consul Xue Erfo first interrogated Ba Delie, questioning whether he had killed the Chinese woman and stating that the evidence was conclusive and that he should confess the truth. Ba Delie, knowing that he could not deny the charges, spoke frankly and appeared calm and not afraid. Ba Delie confessed that he had indeed killed the Chinese woman Zhang Cailian. The murder occurred around midnight on August 4, approximately 12:00 a.m. The location of the murder was upstairs in the house at No. 15 Jiaxing Road. Zhang Cailian was killed by being struck in the head with an ice-breaking tool. When Zhang Cailian cried for help, he used a pillow from the bed to cover her mouth, preventing her from making any sound. As a result, the woman died within a few minutes.

(Moving the Body and Packing It into a Box) Ba Delie also confessed that after killing Zhang on the night of the 4th, he did not sleep that night and stayed in the same room with the female corpse. At dawn, he went out and bought a suitcase from Sandefang, which he carried back to pack the body. At that time, he was in a state of mental confusion and didn't know what to do. After bringing the suitcase to No. 15 Jiaxing Road and carrying it upstairs, he carried the female corpse into the box. He did this all by himself, without any help from others. After packing the corpse into the box, he hired a rickshaw on the street and ordered the driver to transport it to the Huishan Wharf in Yangshupu. The box was carried out of the house at 12:00 a.m. on August 5 and arrived at the wharf at 1:30 a.m., where it was handed over to a coolie to be sent onto the Shanghai Maru ship.

(Trying to Exonerate His Brother) Ba Delie spoke clearly during his confession, but he was sweating profusely and often wiped his forehead with a towel. Ba Delie said that killing Zhang Cailian was a moment of anger and not premeditated. He also claimed that he bought the suitcase and transported the body all by himself, trying to exonerate his brother Qiu Shifu, saying that his brother did not know about the murder of Zhang. He only met his brother on the road after buying the suitcase on the 5th, and even then, his brother did not know that he was buying the suitcase to transport Zhang's body. The court clerk recorded Ba Delie's confession in detail and read it back to him.

(Interrogation of the Accomplice) After Ba Delie confessed to killing Zhang, the Portuguese Consul showed him a photo of Zhang Cailian (taken by Linghua) and asked him if it was her. Ba Delie replied that it was. He was also asked if he wrote the words on the box, and he replied that he did. Then Ba was taken aside, and his brother, the accomplice Qiu Shifu, was interrogated. Qiu Shifu appeared fearful and terrified during his confession, but he firmly denied any involvement in the case. He said that he only met his younger brother on the afternoon of August 5 and knew nothing about the murder or the transportation of the body. He only knew that his younger brother was moving and helped him carry things. He claimed that he did not go upstairs. He only heard his brother mention the murder of Zhang Cailian after the fact. After he found out, he didn't know what to do and kept it to himself. He absolutely did not participate. At this point, the Portuguese Consul showed him the photo of Zhang Cailian and asked if it was her, and he replied that it was.

(To Be Sent to Macao Soon) Yesterday's interrogation lasted a very long time. When Ba Delie left the Xiamen Road West Prison, his lawyer, Lei Gelun, talked to the two defendants for a long time. At the beginning of the hearing, before Ba Delie had made a confession, the defendant's lawyer stated to the court that the defendant had something to say, and then he gradually confessed to the murder. Now that the case has been investigated, the two defendants are still being held in the West Prison. In the next few days, the Consulate will need to question the witnesses once again before handing the suspect Ba Delie over to Macao for a formal trial by the court.

How Did the Old Beggar Die?

Must await forensic examination to clarify

Beggar's brother claims the Yongtaixiang shop owner beat him to death

Gu Kou (aka White-Eyed Er'er) from Tongzhou, aged 60, made a living by begging. On the 21st of this month at approximately 11:00 a.m., Gu and another beggar named Ying Zhengming were begging for food along Grant Road. Ying was walking in front, and Gu was behind. When they reached the entrance of the Yongtaixiang Paper Shop at No. 142 Grant Road, Gu intended to beg from the shop, but unexpectedly collapsed to the ground and lost consciousness. A Chinese constable from Station No. 6 noticed this and immediately sent him to Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment, but the treatment was ineffective, and he died. The Yangshupu Police Station was informed and instructed Detective Ji Xiucheng to investigate. They learned that Gu had died of illness and reported back to the police chief, who instructed the Pushan Villa to bury the body. However, at approximately 8:00 p.m. that evening, the deceased's cousin, Gu Xiaomei, and Ying Zhengming went to the police station and claimed that Gu had been beaten to death by the shop owner and requested an investigation. After a thorough investigation by the police chief, it was determined that there was no evidence to support the claim, and they were dismissed. Gu Xiaomei was still dissatisfied and filed a petition with the First Special District Court Prosecutor's Office on the 24th, requesting a thorough investigation. Chief Prosecutor Wang approved the disinterment for a second autopsy because the case involved a human life. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo Wei, along with Secretary Wang Zuyi, forensic doctors Wei Ligong and Zhang Yan, drove to the forensic examination center on Ferren Road. The Chinese and Western detectives handling the case had already hoisted the coffin containing the body and summoned all the witnesses. Prosecutor Guo first interrogated Gu Xiaomei, who testified, "I did not witness my brother fall. Afterwards, Ying Zhengming informed me that he had been beaten to death by the Yongtaixiang shop owner." Then, Ying Zhengming testified, "Although I was begging in the same place as the deceased, I am blind. After Gu the beggar died, I heard people say that he had been beaten by the shop owner, so I reported it to Gu Xiaomei." Finally, Chinese Constable No. 6 and Western Detective No. 10 arrived to report that they had witnessed the beggar suddenly collapse to the ground and lose consciousness. According to a hawker surnamed Yan, the beggar had fallen on his own and had not been beaten. Prosecutor Guo, after reviewing the testimony, stated that in order to confirm the cause of the beggar's death, it was necessary to reopen the coffin and conduct another autopsy. He asked Gu Xiaomei if he agreed to the re-examination, and Gu expressed extreme approval and personally lifted the coffin lid. Forensic doctors Wei and Zhang immediately began the autopsy, but it could not be completed in a short time. Prosecutor Guo then adjourned the hearing to next Monday, after which he would review the forensic report.

Three Apprentices from Hengfengxin Cotton Cloth Store Commit Suicide Together

All sacrifice themselves due to lack of freedom in marriage

Suicide note says they are determined to commit suicide and should not be searched for

The three have been missing for two days with no news

| Alas, three water ghosts; still people in spring boudoir dreams |

Three apprentices from the Hengfengxin Cotton Cloth Store at No. 109 Wufuli, Tianjin Road, in the Public Concession, usually worked diligently in the store and had no faults. Unexpectedly, on the 25th of this month, they agreed to leave the store without saying goodbye and committed suicide together. Their suicide note said, "We have made up our minds to commit suicide. Please don't look for us, just wait to collect the corpses." The store found the suicide note and reported it to the police station, Public Security Bureau, and Rescue Bureau in the past two days, asking them to be on the lookout. The reasons for the suicide are recorded below. Hengfengxin Cotton Cloth Store is a century-old store. The partners in the store are all old, and there are several apprentices. The three who agreed to commit suicide this time were Pan Songbai, from She County, 21 years old, nearsighted, and always wears glasses, is an only son; Pan Zhanpeng, from She County, 19 years old, with many freckles on his face. The reason for the suicide of these two was that the store checked their family correspondence and found that both were due to lack of freedom in marriage and families that were too old-fashioned, leading to the determination to commit suicide. Another apprentice named Shi Bingnan, also known as Sannan, from Dongting East Mountain, 19 years old, of medium height, speaks Shanghainese, also had the intention of committing suicide due to economic and marital problems. In early July, he took a photo and wrote on the back of the photo, "Alas, three water ghosts; still people in spring boudoir dreams." He also wrote to his mother, saying that men and women are the same and asking her to cultivate his sister to study. What is strange is that the three apprentices left without taking a penny. It has been two days since they left, and there is no news. The store has telegraphed their families to come to Shanghai to search for them.

A Woman on a Tram Exposed Her Deceitful Actions; Many Involved Persons Were Subsequently Arrested

A Wall Collapses in Baoting Lane, Lujiabang, Injuring Many

Yang Cao Suffered the Most Serious Injuries

Baoting Lane in Lujiabang, outside Xiaonanmen in Nanshi, consists of one or two alleyways. Apart from the twenty-odd storefronts along the street, the rest are single or double-story shikumen buildings, totaling dozens of structures. Due to years of neglect, they have become dilapidated. The owner of the lane, Taichang Real Estate Company, originally intended to rebuild new houses, but due to financial constraints, they hired a construction company to repair the buildings to prevent danger. All residents and shopkeepers in the lane were notified and had moved elsewhere. The construction company hired by Taichang Real Estate surrounded the area with bamboo fences and sent a large number of workers to begin repairs. They noticed that a short wall at the No. 57 gate on the south side of the lane needed to be rebuilt because there was a well behind the wall, and water had been seeping into the foundation of the wall for years, causing it to weaken. Yesterday, two bricklayers were assigned to demolish the old wall in order to build a new one. Yang Erfang, a local resident, 61 years old, and his wife, Cao, 54 years old, had only one daughter, Mingzhu, 26 years old, who had been married to Le Genfa from Ningbo through a matchmaker. Because Yang Erfang was old and unable to work, he was supported by his son-in-law and lived with him at No. 2, Lane 60, Yutang Lane. The back building of the house was rented to Yang Yuchun, a Shandong man who ran a sesame cake shop. Yang was 38 years old, his wife, Wang, was 28 years old, and they had two sons, Lianyou, 6 years old, and Liancheng, 2 years old. The back door of their house faced the front door of No. 57 in Baoting Lane. Yesterday morning, Yang Erfang and Yang Yuchun's families were washing clothes or chatting idly at the back door. Two bricklayers were sitting on top of the wall at the No. 57 gate in Baoting Lane, demolishing it. At about 8 o'clock, the short wall, which was about ten feet long, suddenly collapsed. The two bricklayers working on the wall also fell. With a crash, Yang Erfang and others were unable to avoid it and were buried under the wall. The local police station of the First District was notified, and station chief Yi Zuanren arrived at the scene with patrol officers. They quickly rescued the injured men and women from the rubble and transported them to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. The foreman, Zheng Afu, was taken back to the police station for questioning and reported to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation. Among those injured, Yang Cao suffered the most serious injuries and was hospitalized. Yang Erfang suffered a minor leg injury, and Yang Wang and Yang Lianyou suffered minor head injuries. Song Zhang, a woman from Hebei living at No. 1, Lane 60, was also washing clothes there and suffered a minor leg injury. A child, Zhang Dazhai, from No. 57 Wangmiao Street, who was playing there, also suffered a minor head injury. All of them were treated at the hospital and then returned home. The two bricklayers who fell from the wall, Pan Tongsheng and Liu Yusheng, suffered only minor injuries and were discharged from the hospital after treatment and medication.

The Case of New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory Being Sued for Medicinal Narcotics

The Municipal Council's Misunderstanding; The Chamber of Commerce and Others Have Intervened on Their Behalf

New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory has been established for many years and has been registered with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and obtained a license from the Bureau of Health. It has a number of doctors and pharmacists in charge of manufacturing and is a well-known manufacturer of national products. However, at 11:00 AM on the 16th of this month, the Anti-Narcotics Department of the Central Police Station suddenly sent a French detective and a large number of detectives to search the New Asia factory. The factory sent staff to lead them to all parts of the factory, including the narcotics storage room upstairs. There were more than 200 liang of medicinal morphine in the cabinet. The French detective considered it contraband and sent detectives to guard the room. The factory informed them that the stored morphine was used exclusively for making injections and that it was handled in accordance with the regulations of the Bureau of Health for the management of pharmaceutical merchants, and showed the license issued by the Bureau of Health. The French detective then telegraphed a Western chemist from the Municipal Council to come to the factory. The factory's pharmacist explained in detail the various machines and medicines, as well as the purpose and source of the stored medicinal morphine. At 2:00 PM, the French detective took the license, books, invoices, and two liang of morphine to the lawyer, Bo Liang, for consultation, and eventually filed a public prosecution in the Special Court. The factory then entrusted lawyers Jiang Yiping, Zhang Ding, and Tu Zhenhu to defend them. During the court hearing on the 17th, the factory manager strongly argued the following four points: 1. The factory is a legitimate pharmaceutical merchant registered with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and has a pharmaceutical merchant license from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Health. The factory handles narcotics in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Health for the management of pharmaceutical merchants, and their use is exclusively for medical purposes. 2. The factory's narcotics are purchased from French merchants, Baibu Foreign Firm, and other pharmacies. The Customs allows import, and there are books and records to prove it. 3. When the factory sells narcotics, it complies with the regulations of the Customs No. 1300, requiring signatures and seals of formal physicians, pharmacists, and hospitals as proof. 4. Narcotics have great efficacy in medicine, and all modern doctors use them. Before China had its own products, all were supplied by foreign goods. The factory, seeing the importance of this and the purpose of promoting national products, followed legal procedures and the regulations of the Chinese Pharmacopoeia to prepare medicinal narcotic injection solutions in the hope of recovering rights. Now, unfortunately, it has been subject to illegal interference. How painful! If the judge considers the factory's preparation of medicinal narcotic injection solutions to be a crime, then doctors and pharmacists who use narcotics for medical treatment will also be considered illegal, and the cause of new medicine in China will not need to be promoted. It is learned that the Shanghai Medical Association, the New Pharmaceutical Industry Association, and the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce have submitted petitions to the court, arguing reasonably. Attached is the following:

The Shanghai Medical Association submits a document stating that the New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory is operating in accordance with the law and was mistakenly searched by detectives from the police station. The document declares the facts and requests legal release to protect pharmaceutical merchants and promote the industry. Western medicine used to be dependent on foreign countries, with annual imports reaching more than 30 million, a huge loss. Recently, doctors and pharmacists who have studied in various countries have emerged, advocating the self-manufacturing of Western medicines and morphine, and other injection solutions and needle medicines, to meet the needs of treatment and anesthesia for surgery, hoping to recover rights and working hard. It is found that Zhao Rutiao, the chief pharmacist of New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory at No. 1095 Xinzha Road in the city, graduated from the Faculty of Pharmacy of Chiba Medical University in Japan and has specialized knowledge and enthusiasm for manufacturing. Xu Guanqun, the manager of the factory, is strict in management and complies with published regulations. At the beginning of the business, he registered with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and obtained a pharmaceutical merchant license from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Health. The Western medicines produced in large quantities are of many kinds and are manufactured according to new scientific methods. Morphine injection liquid is necessary for medical use. The factory handles it in accordance with Articles 5, 6, and 7 of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Health's regulations for the management of pharmaceutical merchants. All products have been approved by the medical community, and sales in the market are increasing. However, at 11:00 AM on the 16th of this month, (omitted) During the hearing in the Eighth Court, Xu Guanqun stated that he was a legitimate pharmaceutical merchant, that the source of morphine was all purchased from Baibu Foreign Firm, etc., and that it was not sold without the signature of a doctor or formal institution. The French detective present also stated that the statement was true. Judge Liu was understanding and ordered the police station to investigate further and allowed Xu Guanqun to be released on bail pending trial. New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory manufactures Western medicines made by Chinese, and holds a license. The morphine imported is used exclusively for the manufacture of injection solutions and needle medicines and is not used for other purposes or sold separately. It is handled in accordance with the regulations of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Health for the management of pharmaceutical merchants. Western medicine is now popular, and morphine injection solutions and needle medicines are commonly used for the treatment of diseases. The factory's products are used not only by the new medical community in the country but also by the central military medical teams. Therefore, there is no excessive storage of manufacturing raw materials. Although the police station's investigation was the exercise of legitimate authority, this Association believes that the morphine stored by the New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory has an official license and is for legitimate pharmaceutical use. I dare to contribute what I know and submit a public document as proof. I hope that the court will review it and make a judgment as soon as possible, recognizing that the factory's behavior is innocent, so that the truth will be revealed and national Western medicine will be protected. I am grateful and respectfully submit it to Guo of the Shanghai First Special District Local Court.

The Shanghai New Pharmaceutical Industry Association submits a document stating that the pharmaceutical factory is manufacturing in accordance with regulations and was mistakenly searched. The document requests a fair judgment to maintain business operations. The New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory, a member of the Association, has been registered with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and holds a pharmaceutical merchant license from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Health. The new medicines produced are of many kinds and are manufactured according to the ingredients specified in the Chinese Pharmacopoeia. Morphine injection liquid is required for medical use and used to be imported from abroad. Recently, it has also been imitated in order to recover rights. However, at 11:00 AM on the 16th of this month, (omitted) They were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court. The manager explained that the morphine was purchased from French merchants, Baibu Foreign Firm, etc., and that the Customs allowed it to enter the country and there are books and records to prove it. When the manufactured narcotics are sold, they must be certified with a signature and seal by a formal physician, pharmacist, and hospital. Judge Liu was understanding and ordered the police station to investigate further and allowed Xu Guanqun to be released on bail pending trial. The morphine injection needle produced by New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory has remarkable efficacy. Members of the Association purchased it from the factory and resold it to doctors, hospitals, and colleagues in other places. The stored morphine is indeed used for the manufacture of injection solutions and needle medicines. There is no other use, and it is not sold separately. It is handled in accordance with the regulations for the management of pharmaceutical merchants issued by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Health. These morphine injection needle medicines are essential for pain relief after external surgery and bullet wounds. Therefore, the military hospitals under the central government also often purchase them from the factory. Although the police station's investigation was the exercise of legitimate authority, it was filed due to a misunderstanding that it had other functions. The Association clearly understands the history of the factory and dares to guarantee that the stored morphine is entirely for legitimate pharmaceutical use. I hereby respectfully present the facts and request that the court review them and issue a fair reply as soon as possible to maintain business operations for the public convenience. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai First Special District Local Court.

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce writes: On the 23rd of this month, a letter was received from the New Pharmaceutical Industry Association stating that a letter had been received from the New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory, a member of the Association (omitted). The New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory manufactures injection solutions for the purpose of promoting the independence and self-sufficiency of new medicines. The morphine used for all injection solutions is purchased from French merchants, Baibu Foreign Firm, and various pharmacies. The Customs allows it to enter the country and there are proof. Its sale is also handled in accordance with Article 7 of the regulations for the management of pharmaceutical merchants issued by the department. The only question at present is the third item of Article 3 of the Regulations on the Management of Narcotics. However, the morphine mentioned above is not self-made. The pharmaceutical factory only prepares it according to the Chinese Pharmacopoeia. It does not seem to involve the regulatory norms of the special manufacturing law. I hereby prepare a letter of proof and respectfully request that the court uphold justice in order to maintain the foundation of independent Western medicine for the public good. It would be appreciated if you could correct the report accordingly. Respectfully addressed to the editor-in-chief of the Shen Bao Newspaper, August 26th.

Page 17

Spring and Autumn

The Symbol of Fighting

— Si Su

I remember seeing a very common fight when I was little. A small street vendor selling fruit was trying to sell his goods when a burly man with a menacing face came and wanted to buy fruit from him. After the vendor named a price, the man only offered half. The vendor refused to sell, but the man insisted. After a few words, the man suddenly became furious and threw the selected fruit onto the street. The vendor did not get angry, but only asked for money. The man's face turned even redder, and he kicked over the fruit basket, causing the fruit inside to roll out. The vendor then grabbed the man and started arguing loudly, and soon a crowd gathered to watch the commotion. However, the man was strong and muscular, while the vendor was thin and frail, so he was no match. After being punched and kicked by the man, the vendor was knocked to the ground like the fruit in the basket. Suddenly, someone nearby became indignant and stepped forward to grab the man, asking why he was using his strength to bully others. They disagreed, and a fight broke out between them. This person was about as strong as the man, and they were evenly matched, fighting fiercely. The vendor had already gotten up from the ground, initially with a tearful face. Later, seeing the two men fighting intensely, he stood there foolishly, watching as if he found it very interesting. He even forgot that the fight had started because of him and forgot about the fruit and the basket rolling on the ground. By the time the fight was over and the crowd dispersed, the fruit had been trampled and the basket had been flattened.

This scene is symbolic of the case of the nine small islands of Yuehai being occupied by France. Our Ministry of Foreign Affairs only issued a few protests when the news first came out. Later, when Japan came forward, it took the lead by occupying the islands, thus lodging a de facto protest. Our country then adopted a wait-and-see attitude. As a result, almost all the reports in the newspapers in the past half-month regarding this case have been about the arguments between Paris and Tokyo. Apart from telegrams from civil organizations requesting the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to fight for the cause, there was no other news from our country.

The result of waiting and seeing will probably not deviate from the precedent of the fruit being trampled and the basket being flattened. Reuters has already told us that the Parisian officials are mostly silent about the Japanese representative's declaration to avoid escalating the situation. However, the French government may allow respect for Japan's economic interests while rejecting Japan's claim to political sovereignty. Naturally, it is not as easy to knock over an opponent who is about as strong as you are, as it is to knock over a thin and frail opponent.

Random Chat, Cartoons

Would You Rather Be a Rich Family's Dog Than a Human Child?

— Qian Yun Writes, Wen Liang Draws

The children of the Yang family suffer along with their father because he cannot earn money. Not to mention that they don't have the opportunity to study and learn to read, as there are countless children in China who are out of school. However, they are hungry several times a day, which is a problem they must solve every day. They are so hungry that tears stream from their eyes, but their father says he has no choice! Sometimes he even scolds them, and sometimes he hugs them and cries with them. The children's eyes narrow into slits when they cry, while the father's eyes widen like copper bells!

Believe it or not, the foreign dog of the Liu family has won the favor of its owner. Not only is it fed a dollar's worth of beef every day, but once when it was sick for a month, a famous veterinarian was hired. After daily diagnosis and treatment, the medical bill came to over two thousand five hundred taels, perhaps because the veterinarian was so famous. Narrow-minded friends cannot help but ask why he is willing to spend so much money on a dog. He replies: "There's no other reason, it's just that it's 'extremely clever'." This is not a problem for a rich family. Moreover, the Liu family probably also does a lot of good deeds worth tens of millions. However, compared to the children of the Yang family, it is still an absolutely wonderful contrast.

From this perspective, one can say that calling someone a "dog" is not necessarily an exclusively insulting term.

Under the Thighs

— Rong Yu

The times are constantly advancing. Our secret history has gone from pomegranate skirts to long cheongsams to bare thighs.

These thighs, with their smooth skin, curving lines, stepping on high heels, slightly revealed beneath the long cheongsam, are so alluring! So sensual! Even if you are Liu Xiahui, even if you are a man of Lu, even if you are an old Confucian scholar eating cold meat in Sanjiacun, even if you are an old eunuch in the past palace, you still have to take the opportunity to glance at them a few times. I have never heard of anyone who glances at them without feeling a sense of infatuation and distraction.

Since thighs have such charm, any film that has a few pairs of plump, white, and tender thighs captured in the lens will be able to sell seats and satisfy people's appetites. The star dancers in dance troupes must publicly bare their jade legs to captivate and inspire people, causing them to drool. The condition for modern women is to bare their legs under long cheongsams. Thighs! Bare thighs! They are the pride of the twentieth century. How many people have fallen for them, praised them, pursued them, and even sacrificed everything for them. And the harvest under the thighs is money, jewels, clothing, and everything else. There are also countless toads staring with their eyes wide open and their bellies bulging, worshiping under the thighs. The power of the thighs is great! The vast majority of beings chant in unison: "Great! Great!"

X X X X

The same thighs, different values. The thighs of country folk.

X X X X

The same thighs, different loves and hates. Those powdered and jade-like thighs, which are also thighs that consume and distribute profit, are pursued and worshiped. Those thighs covered in mud are also thighs that are powerful for production, but they are disgusted and despised. Alas! This is also the mystery of the times!

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Fourteen: Difficulties in Finding a Wife, Hesitant and Anxious About the Future, Inviting Friends for a Small Gathering, Shyly Recalling Past Events

Ms. Jiang said, "Cousin, since you have something to do, you don't have to stay here today. You can go back to the camp for now, and we can talk another day." Guan Yaowu stood up and laughed! "To be honest, as long as Aunt has a word, I will have fulfilled my responsibility. As for talking today or another day, I don't mind." After saying this, he went to the Zhao family in the backyard with a smile. Old Man Zhao briefly told Guan Yaowu about the situation in the past two days, which made him even more confident that the matter had a high chance of success. He returned to the camp with abundant joy. As soon as he entered the company headquarters, Zhao Ziqiang followed him in and laughed, "Brother, how is it going? There shouldn't be any problems, right?" Guan Yaowu slowly took off his military cap and placed it on the small table, looking at Zhao Ziqiang with a faint smile on his face. Zhao Ziqiang said, "What are you smiling at? It's just marrying a wife and raising children. Who doesn't do that? There's nothing to laugh about." Guan Yaowu laughed, "I'm not laughing at anything else. I'm laughing at you for celebrating your eightieth birthday on New Year's Eve, running into such a commotion. Any other time would have been fine to talk about a wife, but you just had to run into the day of this grand review. You have to take care of both official and private matters. I had to pay out of my own pocket to buy white sheets because there weren't enough. Now I'm going to be in debt again. Review, review. The commotion is making people suffer. You still have the energy to think about a wife." Zhao Ziqiang said, "What can we do if we run into this day? I think our battalion is also short of too many people. Otherwise, we could learn from the First Battalion and borrow people from other companies. That would be the best way. If a company is short thirty people, we can report ten or eight people as orderlies, and then borrow twenty people to make up the numbers. No one will know. These new recruits we temporarily hired are killing us to train." Guan Yaowu sighed and said, "These committee officials only look at the surface. What can we do? (170)"

Children's Paradise

Summer Retreat

— Yan

The setting sun was swallowed up by the Western Hills, and the slender willow branches were hung with a plain moon. At the same time, the summer heat was taken away by the red sun, and cool breezes came with the plain moon. The children, having finished their meals and bathed, came to the alley to enjoy the cool air and play. Because they saw each other every night, they were as close as siblings. They put their arms around each other's shoulders, held hands, sang and danced together, played the harmonica, and played hide-and-seek. Often, they were so happy that they forgot to go to bed until late at night, and their mothers and sisters had to come and take them home one by one. One evening, on a bright moonlit night, after they had jumped and laughed for a while, Xiumei gathered everyone and suggested, "We play like this every day, and it feels a bit boring. Tonight, I want to change things up and have a summer retreat. I don't know if everyone agrees." Qiuxia was the first to shout, "I agree! Raise your hand!" She also asked, "How exactly will this retreat be held?" Xiumei then said, "Let's each sing and tell stories, but they must contain a cold meaning, so that everyone who hears them will feel cool." Everyone cheered, "That's really interesting! Come on! Come on!"

Xiumei was the initiator and was chosen to go first. She was already in junior high school and was a grown-up. She stood up gracefully and said, "Dear children! Yesterday, I went to the Northeast. Changbai Mountain was covered in white snow. The cold wind howled, and it was so cold that my nose almost fell off. I walked north through the wind and snow, shrinking my hands and neck. When I arrived at the Songhua River, I saw that the wide river had turned into a flat road. It had actually frozen into thick ice. Long-distance buses were running back and forth on it. I felt strange, so I walked up to it. But I lost my footing and fell. When I opened my eyes, I was lying in bed. It was just a dream!" Everyone said, "Cold! Cold! The Northeast is so cold!"

The second one was Little Goryeo. He was a Korean, so everyone gave him this nickname. He sang mischievously, "The cold wind is blowing, the cold rain is bleak." He sang clearly and melodiously, and it was very cold. Everyone clapped and said, "The Cold Clothes Song is well sung! Sing on!" But he said with a grin, "It's not cold below, so I won't sing anymore." So everyone said, "Little Goryeo, you're a bad egg."

"The accumulated snow buries the instep, the firm ice is on the beard, the fierce birds leave their nests, the horses hesitate, the monk's cotton robe is not warm, the fingers crack the skin," Chun Guan, who had read the lament for ancient battlefields, recited the above sentences. Some people clamored that they didn't understand, so Xiumei stood up and explained them to them. Everyone said, "This kind of fighting is really freezing people to death!"

Xuezhen stood up and said, "Last winter, I brought a piece of ice back from outside, and when I got home, I broke it into pieces on the ground. My little brother saw the ice sugar all over the ground and grabbed it to eat it. But when he put it in his mouth, he opened his mouth and cried, and I laughed. Everyone laughed, 'Frozen to death, the retribution for being greedy.'"

Xiao Mao wanted to speak a long time ago. Now it was his turn, and he jumped up and said, "Have you ever heard of someone freezing to death in June?" Everyone said, "Stop talking nonsense!" He said, "Who's talking nonsense? The teacher told us about it. During the Qing Dynasty, there was a Xue Fucheng, and the emperor sent him to foreign countries to investigate. When he came back to Guangdong, it was the month of June, and it was unbearably hot. The Guangdong officials, because he was an imperial envoy, tried their best to entertain him and specially built an ice room for him to live in. But it was too cold, and he got sick and died. So everyone said that Xue Fucheng was frozen to death in June." The children said in unison, "Strange, strange! Interesting, interesting!"

Xin Nv only read in the first grade, and she also stood up and said, "Snowflakes fly, dogs are happy." Everyone laughed, "Xin Nv is also happy."

A Fu was used to reading idle books at the small book stall at the alley entrance. When it was his turn, he blurted out, "In the twelfth month, snowflakes fly, Meng Jiangnu goes out to deliver cold clothes." When he sang to this point, he laughed before everyone else did.

Finally, it was Xi Liang's turn. I don't know when he got a handful of white paper scraps. He stood up and pretended to be frightened and said, "It's snowing outside!" Everyone really looked out of the alley. Taking advantage of this, he grabbed a handful of shredded paper and scattered it upwards, shouting, "The snow is so heavy!" The paper scraps fell piece by piece, and everyone really thought it was snowing, so they grabbed low stools and ran home. Seeing everyone running away, he laughed heartily. It turned out that everyone had heard so many cold songs and stories, and their minds had already changed, so when they saw white flakes falling from above, they thought it was really snowing.

Xiumei said, "It's getting late, everyone else has gone home, we should also go to sleep and see you tomorrow!" So everyone went home happily. Suddenly, the alley was silent, and only the bright moon was still shining brightly, and the clear wind was still blowing gently.

New Opening Chapter for the Double Seventh Festival

— Zhang Mengfei

The seventh day of the seventh month is today. The Weaver Girl and the Cowherd meet on the Magpie Bridge.

The Milky Way is full of moonlight. The wind is calm and there are few waves. The two meet and talk a lot of love. The autumn weather is pleasant and carefree. Weaver Girl, this year we are happy to celebrate the National Goods Year. Your clothes are definitely fashionable national goods. You advocate for the recovery of rights. I admire my wife as a patriotic female compatriot. Your bust is prominent and your legs are exposed in a modern style. You are especially beautiful compared to those years. Thinking that we have been apart for a year and meet today. Tonight is once a year. Cowherd, the country is in turmoil and it is difficult to find fun. China is really too bad. Although the northeast situation has subsided, it is a pity that the four provinces are already unstable. Let's wait until next year to order the Taoyao again. Oh, Weaver Girl, tonight we can only talk about romance. Why bother talking about national affairs? At this moment, the Cowherd wants to hug your slender waist. Educational News

Important News

Experts to Edit Syllabi for Vocational Courses

Vocational School Graduates Will Also Take Entrance Examinations

The Ministry of Education has convened meetings multiple times to formulate and announce curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools. It will also begin to invite experts to organize a drafting committee to revise the curriculum standards for normal schools, so that normal schools across the country will have a basis to follow and seek uniformity. However, vocational schools have never had concrete curriculum standards since their establishment. Because vocational school curricula and levels are extremely inconsistent, it is difficult to set a common standard for all schools to follow uniformly. However, primary and secondary schools already have curriculum standards, and normal schools will also have entrance examinations in the future after curriculum standards are formulated, so that they can be promoted to higher education. How can vocational schools be unique? Therefore, vocational curricula must eventually be appropriately summarized and analyzed to gradually concretize them in order to seek universal adaptation. It is reported that the Ministry of Education will not organize a separate committee for the editing of vocational curricula. Instead, it will send letters to scholars and experts from vocational schools across the country, requesting them to draft outlines of various vocational curricula separately. The Ministry of Education will gather opinions and make a final decision. It is also reported that the Ministry of Education is also planning to carry out this matter.

Ministry of Education Orders Luo Jialun to Rectify National Central University

(Nanjing, 26th) The Ministry of Education, in response to Luo Jialun's request to investigate the declaration issued by the alumni association of the former National Southeastern University, National Higher Normal School, and National Central University, which contained attacks, specifically instructed the president of the university to state that the attached slanderous writings not only confused the public and violated criminal law, but inevitably contained the intention to incite turmoil and disregard the government's repeated orders to rectify education. Since the president's appointment, his achievements have been remarkable, and all facilities and financial matters have been legally approved by the Ministry and government agencies at any time. In addition to the Ministry taking measures to investigate and prohibit the dissemination of the writings, the president is instructed to pay close attention to the order within the school, make every effort to rectify it, and the request to thoroughly investigate the truth should not be considered.

Ministry of Education Orders Three Private Universities in Beiping to Close

(Nanjing, 26th) Recently, the Ministry of Education found that the three schools of Yuwen University, Pingmin University, and North China University in Beiping [Peiping] had incomplete subjects and inadequate facilities, affecting the studies of students in North China. It ordered the schools to stop recruiting new students and to carry out closure procedures.

Detailed Report on the Annual Meeting of the Science Society of China

Opening Ceremony: Chairman He Lu, Wu Liande, and others deliver speeches

Election: Xi Wenhao, Zhao Yuanren, and seven others elected as this year's directors

Proposal: Sichuan authorities urged to organize a committee for surveying and utilizing abundant resources

Request: The government should use scientific talent to improve national medicine

The 18th Annual Meeting of the Science Society of China commenced on the 17th of this month in Sichuan Province. A group of over seventy members, including Bing Xin, Wu Liande, Yang Xiaoying, Ding Xielin, and Hu Gangfu, traveled to Sichuan on a special ship, the Minquan, on the 5th of this month. When the ship arrived in Hankou, they were hosted by member Zhang Yanxiang for a tour of Wuhan University. Upon arriving in Wanxian, they were welcomed with a banquet by Division Commander Wang Fangzhou and various sectors. Arriving in Chongqing, they were greeted by representatives from the county government and the press, and at 6 PM on the 15th, they arrived safely in Chongqing.

Liu Xiang Hosts a Banquet: Upon arrival in Chongqing, representatives from the local military, political, business, and academic circles, including Lu Zuofu and He Beiheng, totaling over fifty people, greeted the members with military music and firecrackers. All members, along with eighty members from Sichuan Province, boarded the Minyue ship and sailed up the Jialing River to the Baxian Middle School for lodging. Although the members had endured a long and arduous journey of ten days in hot weather, their spirits remained high and showed no signs of fatigue. Registration took place on the morning of the 16th, with 516 members actually present. In the afternoon, representatives Wang Jiliang, Bing Nongshan, Yang Yunzhong, and Zhou Zijing visited the military headquarters. That evening, Governor Liu Xiangcheng hosted a banquet at Taoyuan, represented by Gan Dianyi, the head of the political affairs department. During the banquet, there was detailed discussion on scientific construction in Sichuan Province and the development of its abundant resources. Everyone felt the pain of the loss of the eastern provinces and recognized the urgent need to develop Sichuan.

Annual Meeting Opens: The opening ceremony of the 18th Annual Meeting was held on the morning of the 17th at the Eastern Sichuan Normal School. Chairman He Lu, representatives from various institutions, and members delivered sincere speeches. All major newspapers in the city printed red reports to express their welcome. In the afternoon at 4 PM, lectures were held in three locations. At the Youth Association, Dr. Wu Liande spoke on "Health, Wealth, and Life," and female member Dr. Ma Xinyi spoke on "Plants and Life." At the General Chamber of Commerce, Dr. Hu Buzeng spoke on "A Discussion of the Problem of Rural Economic Revival in Sichuan." At the Eastern Sichuan Normal School, Dr. Bing Nongshan spoke on "Biology and Science Education." Each location attracted five to six hundred attendees, demonstrating great enthusiasm. The interest of the people of Sichuan in science was evident. In the evening, over fifty organizations from the city hosted a banquet for all members at the Shizhong Garden.

Society Affairs Meeting: On the morning of the 18th, all members traveled to Wenquan Park on Minsheng ships, where they were hosted by the Western China Academy. At 4 PM, a society affairs meeting was held, chaired by Yang Yunzhong, who reported on the work of the Science Society of China over the past year. Zhou Zijing then reported on the economic situation and accounts, and He Dekui, the auditing representative, explained that everything was accurate and unanimously accepted. The chairman further explained the source of the funds and expressed special gratitude to Song Hanzhang, Cai Yuanpei, and Xu Xinliu, the three trustees, for their proper management. Member Liu Mengxi proposed that Mr. Yang Xingfo had made great contributions to the society and, unfortunately, met an untimely death. The entire conference should stand in silence for three minutes. The proposal was unanimously approved, and everyone stood in silence to express their condolences. Pei Jian then reported on the status of the Biological Research Institute on behalf of Bing Nongshan, the director of the institute. Wang Jiliang reported on the situation of the editorial department, and the chairman reported on the situation of the library on behalf of Lu Jine, the librarian. Finally, Xu Nairen, the representative of the election committee, reported the results of the election of new directors. Xi Wenhao, Zhao Yuanren, Ren Hongjun, Zhu Kezhen, Ye Zhi, Hu Gangfu, and Li Siguang were elected as this year's directors. The meeting adjourned at 6 PM.

Important Proposals: On the morning of the 19th, all members traveled to Jinyun Mountain in one hundred and twenty sedan chairs. At 2 PM, the second society affairs meeting was held in the auditorium of Jinyun Temple. Tang Yue, He Lu, and Liu Mengxi were elected as the degree adjudication committee for the afternoon, and He Dekui and Gu Jigao were elected as auditors for the next year. Wang Jiliang was elected as the editor-in-chief for the next year, and He Lu, Ren Hongjun, Wu De, Hu Xiansu, Xu Nairen, Liu Mengxi, Ge Suiren, and Lu Zuofu were elected as editors. Next, the society's constitution was amended to add the clause "The board of directors shall establish seven standing directors," which was passed. Then, six proposals were discussed. ⑴ Hu Sheng submitted a proposal co-signed by Hu Boyuan and twelve others, suggesting that the Sichuan authorities organize a Sichuan Abundant Resources Survey and Utilization Committee, which was passed. ⑵ Zeng Jifu and others submitted a proposal co-signed by Ma Xinyi and sixteen others, stating that the Department of Biology of the College of Science at Henan University was ordered to be suspended. They requested assistance, and three representatives were appointed to handle the case. ⑶ Wu Liande submitted a proposal co-signed by Bing Zhi and seven others, requesting that the government use scientific talent to improve and reorganize national medicine, which was passed. ⑷ Ye Shanding submitted a proposal co-signed by Li Zhenpian and eight others, requesting that the society jointly establish a Chinese Pharmaceutical Research Institute with the Chinese Medical Association and other organizations, which was passed. ⑸ Sheng Shaozhang submitted a Chengdu-Chongqing Railway project plan co-signed by Sun Pinke and four others, proposing that the Science Society of China suggest that the Sichuan Provincial authorities prioritize the construction, which was passed. The plan was handed over to the representative to present. ⑹ Ma Shouzheng, Chen Yanshan, and others proposed that the Science Society of China should organize an Agricultural Committee to use scientific methods to promote Chinese agriculture, which was passed. Three committee members were elected to liaise with the society's board of directors on organizational matters. Finally, a motion was passed to send letters of thanks to the various institutions and individuals who hosted the annual meeting, and a motion was passed to present a permanent commemorative item to the Western China Academy. The meeting adjourned, and it was already late at night when they returned to the hot springs.

Reading Papers: On the morning of the 20th, papers were read in the temporary auditorium of Wenquan Park, with over one hundred people in attendance. The papers presented at this annual meeting included Bing Zhi's "Invertebrates of the Lower Yangtze River," Ma Shouzheng's "Research on Phosphorus," Pei Jian's "Outline of Nanjing Plants," Zeng Jifu's "Research on Henan Salamanders," He Kuiyuan's "New Teaching Methods for Intermediate Mathematics," Zheng Wanjun's "Outline of Chinese Pines," Zhu Xi's "Evolution of Chemical Biology," Fang Bingwen's "Records of New Genera of Cyprinidae in Western China," Jin Lanyuan Rongfu's "Chemical Composition and Physiological Function of Sheep Horn Plate," Ye Dingzhi's "On Chinese Medicines," Hu Ze's "Research on Sichuan's Huangge Pulp," and Wang Shanshen's "New Interpretation of the Branching Habits of Cotton Crops," totaling forty-one papers. All were the result of the members' daily research. There were twelve papers read by Japanese scholars. There were questions and discussions on each, and the interest was very strong. In the afternoon, they went to the Beibei field to visit the new planting projects. At 5 PM, there was a public lecture. Ma Shouzheng spoke on "From Fertilizer to Rural Revival," Chen Yanshan spoke on "The Importance of Improving Chinese Cotton," and Yongzhen spoke on "Improvement of Sericulture." There were over four hundred attendees. This society's meeting in Sichuan made an excellent impression. The people of Sichuan eagerly hoped to use the power of scientists to shift the political mentality and move towards peace and construction. The governor is now in Chengdu and has sent a special telegram welcoming all members to visit. They are currently preparing vehicles, and the members of the society are also organizing various activities such as investigations, studies, and lectures, and are departing for Chengdu.

Wang Jiyuan Returns to Shanghai from Fujian

Bringing Back Dozens of Views of the Min River

Jiang Guangding Commissions Wang to Paint Murals

The famous painter Wang Jiyuan went to Fujian at the beginning of the month at the invitation of Zheng Zhenwen, the Director of Education of Fujian, to hold a solo painting exhibition for the opening of the new building of the Fuzhou Branch of the Chinese Arts and Crafts Society. He was very welcomed by people from all walks of life in the province. During his trip, Wang, appreciating the beauty of the Min River scenery, made great efforts to create works in the clear weather, rain, morning, and evening, writing dozens of oil paintings, watercolor paintings, and ink paintings of the three mountains in Fuzhou City, ⑴ Yu Mountain, ⑵ Ping Mountain, ⑶ Wushi Mountain, and Cangqian Mountain in Nantai, and Songquan of Gu Mountain, the peaks of Gu Ridge, the ships of Mawei, and the clear currents of Hongshan. Jiang Guangnai, the chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government, admired Wang's works very much and specially commissioned Wang to paint four murals for the Provincial Government: ⑴ Yu Mountain White Pagoda, ⑵ Yongquan of Gu Mountain, ⑶ Hongshan of Min River, ⑷ Luo Shengtower of Mawei. The specified format is very large. Wang has returned to Shanghai by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Taishun ship yesterday (26th). It is reported that he brought back dozens of new works of the Min River scenery as a reference for making murals.

Huadong Women's Middle School Opens

Ten High School Tuition Waivers Offered

Huadong Women's Middle School on Beile Road in this city has been established for two years, and the results have been remarkable. The number of students this semester has exceeded four hundred. The school is scheduled to open on the 28th of this month, and registration has already begun yesterday. In order to provide opportunities for girls from poor families to complete high school, the school has specially set up ten high school tuition waivers. Girls from poor families who are interested in attending can apply to the school through a qualified guarantor. It is also reported that in order to enable graduates of the normal and business departments to meet the needs of society and promote the employment of graduates, the school is working hard to connect with various educational groups and industries.

Rotary Cup: China Still Able to Retain Championship in Shanghai International Tennis

Yesterday's Doubles: China Wins Straight Sets Against Portugal in Three

Corlachea Wins 3-1 Against Wang Wenzheng

Today: Zheng Zhaojia in Dramatic Battle Against Corlachea

Wang Wenzheng to Play Against Xun Na: Expected to Win

Wang Wenzheng embraced a do-or-die spirit yesterday, hoping to subdue Corlachea in one fell swoop, but his fierce strokes were all broken by Corlachea. As a result, Wang's plan failed, and he ultimately lost. Corlachea won the fourth set with a score of 9-7, adding up to the results of the match held the previous day. Corlachea won with scores of 6-3, 6-4, 0-6, 9-7.

Yesterday was the second day of the Robertson Cup Shanghai International Tennis Tournament. In addition to the match between Corlachea and Wang, which was not completed due to darkness on the first day and was continued yesterday, the main match was doubles. Both matches were very important, and the outcome of the match between Corlachea and Wang Wenzheng was of particular concern to the audience. Therefore, the China Tennis Court was even more crowded yesterday, and people did not fear the scorching sun.

In the doubles match, China still consisted of the old partners Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang. Portugal's lineup was still S Corlachea and Kosta. At the start, the Portuguese players were very sharp. In addition, Zheng Zhaojia's hand movements were not smooth, and he frequently lost points, while Yu Tianguang's work in front of the net was excellent, and his strokes were very sharp, greatly praised by the audience. Portugal took the lead with 4-2. Later, Zheng gradually recovered his original state, and finally won with 6-4, reversing the defeat. In the second and third sets, Yu Tianguang was still strong and did not decrease in the slightest. Zheng Zhaojia's hand movements gradually became skilled, and his sharpness gradually emerged. His serve was most praised. The two cooperated skillfully and defended the net firmly, winning three consecutive sets, with scores of 6-4, 6-3, 6-2.

Chinese doubles players Zheng Zhaojia (right) and Yu Tianguang (left)

(Photo by Qichang)

Today is the last two singles matches. There is no question that China will retain the championship. Although Wang Wenzheng lost one singles match to Corlachea, he can steadily win against Xun Na. Since the doubles match was won by China yesterday, China has steadily taken three groups. Portugal's hopes are completely extinguished. However, the outcome of today's match between Zheng Zhaojia and Corlachea, although it does not affect the championship, the performance of the two is worth noting. Corlachea once defeated Machida, a Shanghai intercity player from Japan, in the preliminary round, and also won 3-1 against Wang Wenzheng. In the preliminary round of the senior singles, Corlachea also defeated Liang Deguang, with a score of 3-2. Zheng Zhaojia once defeated Liang Deguang in the Youyou Cup, but lost to Wang Wenzheng in the final of the China Open singles. Based on this record, it is unknown who will win between Corlachea and Zheng. But in terms of hitting method, Zheng Zhaojia seems to be able to beat Corlachea. What will happen after all, viewers are waiting to see.

Corlachea Actually Wins

(Wang Wenzheng's Wisdom and Strategies Exhausted) The match between Wang and Corlachea was not able to finish the other day, the score being 3-6, 4-6, 6-0, 6-6. Yesterday at 3:30 PM, the game continued. Wang, for the sake of caution, specially arrived at the court in advance to practice with others to loosen his wrists and to boost morale. The original referee was Bode, but he was unable to come due to personal reasons, so Jiang Daozhang took his place. The linesmen were also replaced by two people. After the start of the match, Wang launched lightning-like strokes, breaking Corlachea's serve. The audience was delighted by this. Unexpectedly, Wang's serve was easily lost, making the score 7-7. Corlachea proceeded cautiously, using a slice to obtain a dangerous opportunity, but things did not go as desired. With one or two strokes, Corlachea finally won this game and this set and this match. During the match, when Wang's ball went out of bounds, the linesman yelled, but Corlachea also made a "out of bounds" sound at the same time, which was not appropriate.

Doubles Match Won Back by China

(Yu Tianguang Particularly Pleasing) Portugal, after Corlachea's win in singles, quite wanted to get their hands on the championship. If the Portuguese team had won the doubles and Corlachea also won against Zheng Zhaojia, they would have high hopes for winning the championship. However, whether Corlachea can win against Zheng Zhaojia is questionable. The Portuguese doubles team is not a first-rate team, so their hopes are just dreams. After the beginning, because of Zheng Zhaojia's frequent mistakes, the Portuguese players got the upper hand, taking the lead with 3-1 and 4-2. However, Zheng and Yu broke this later, taking three consecutive sets. Yu Tianguang's performance in this match was particularly pleasing. His skills in front of the net were excellent. Whether it was high pressure or low blocking, he was very confident. He often attacked the opponent's backhand, and every move was surprisingly effective, winning great praise from the audience. Zheng Zhaojia was mediocre. He made more mistakes in the first set. From the second set to the third set, Zheng gradually recovered his original state. His serve was as heavy as a cannonball, and his blocking was also measured. He also shot balls sharp as arrows towards the boundary, and he received much praise from the audience. But it is a strange thing that Zheng and Yu are both good at backhand strokes, but often make mistakes in forehands.

(Straight Sets, Easy and Comfortable) The Portuguese players took the lead. Corlachea obtained the serve. Zheng Zhaojia also obtained the serve. The Portuguese players then added two more games, making the score 3-1, then 4-2. The Portuguese players were very imposing. The audience was amazed by this. But looking at their performance, it is difficult for them to win the final victory. Therefore, the next four games were won by Zheng and Yu, ending with 6-4. In the second set, after Kosta won the serve, Zheng and Yu added three consecutive games. Then each won with their serve, making the score 5-3. The Chinese team broke Kosta's serve again, winning the set again with 6-3. In the third set, Zheng and Yu were in full bloom. Corlachea only obtained his two serves, and all the rest belonged to China. China then won again with 6-2.

Chinese YMCA Open Swim Finals Tonight

Five New Records Set in Yesterday's Preliminary Rounds

Boys' Group 40-Yard Breaststroke Also Breaks Record

| Adult, Women's, and Boys' Groups Compete Fiercely Tonight

The Shanghai Chinese YMCA's seventh open swimming competition began last night. At the beginning of the opening ceremony, the association's new general secretary, Lu Ganchen, delivered an opening speech amid applause, saying that the large number of participants in this competition is the highest in history, and swimming has gradually become popular. Its success can be foreseen.

Only one final was held last night, with the rest being preliminary rounds, resulting in five new records. The finals of the three groups will be held tonight, and better results are expected.

Finals Break Records

Yesterday's only final was the Boys' Group (B) 40-yard breaststroke. Hu Qijie, who holds the tournament record of 35.6 seconds, was also one of the competitors. The surrounding situation was very noticeable. It was hoped that this child who holds the tournament record would show something. As the crowd's emotions were high, the one who broke through the waves and landed on the other shore first was actually the boy the audience was eagerly anticipating. His result was 33.2 seconds, breaking his own record. There was a loud applause that lasted for a long time. This was one of the most exciting scenes in the competitions last night. The final results are as follows:

40-yard Breaststroke: 1) Hu Qijie 2) Hu Qixiong 3) Zhu Dacheng 33.2 seconds

Five New Records Set

The preliminary results were quite impressive. Three new tournament records were set in the five preliminary events for the adult group, including: 1) Chen Yuquan's 6 minutes and 20 seconds in the 400-yard freestyle, breaking his own tournament record of 6 minutes and 28 seconds; 2) Yin Yanjun's 1 minute and 8.6 seconds in the 100-yard freestyle, breaking his own tournament record of 1 minute and 10.6 seconds; 3) Hu Xiangbi's 1 minute and 30.6 seconds and Zhou Ruiqin's 1 minute and 32.8 seconds in the 100-yard backstroke, both breaking Ling Chongju's tournament record of 1 minute and 35.8 seconds. The boys' group also set two new records: 1) Chen Hongming's 31.4 seconds, Zhang Huabang's 35.2 seconds, and Zhu Daoliang's 35.4 seconds in the 40-yard breaststroke, all breaking Hu Qijie's tournament record of 35.8 seconds; 2) Liang Yousheng's 1 minute and 24 seconds and Li Tie's 1 minute and 34 seconds in the 100-yard freestyle, both breaking Wu Zhili's tournament record of 1 minute and 35 seconds. Hu Qijie's 33.2 seconds in the Boys' Group (B) 40-yard breaststroke final broke his own tournament record of 35.8 seconds.
